# Skyrim:Riverwood Trader

## Overview

The Riverwood Trader

The **Riverwood Trader** is a small general trade store located in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

The store sells a variety of weapons, clothes, armor, and other items. It is run by local shopkeeper, [Lucan Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius"), and his sister, [Camilla Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius"). Lucan usually displays a beloved [Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") decoration on the counter. When you first encounter them, the claw has been stolen by the thief [Arvel the Swift](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").

If anything happens to Lucan, Camilla will take over running the store. If they both die, it will be abandoned completely.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |

\* Only becomes a merchant if Lucan Valerius is dead.

## Related Quests

- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").
- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.

### Riverwood Trader

Riverwood Trader downstairs

In front of the shop are some piles of firewood, several barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), and a cart filled with [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). At the rear are a flight of wooden stairs leading to the balcony above.

In the southern corner of the downstairs room is an L-shaped counter which Lucan stands behind when he is in the store. In addition to the [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) there are four loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins on the countertop as well as the [Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw"), once you have retrieved it. Under the counter is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and hanging from the ceiling are two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid and a rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Against the southwest wall is a cupboard and set of shelves filled with more displayed merchandise, while against the northwest wall is a barrel, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Opposite the front door is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front of it. In front of the fireplace is a round wooden table and chair where Camilla sometimes sits when she is in the store. There are two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a wedge of cheese on top of the table.

To the left of the fireplace is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") with a food barrel underneath and a set of shelves to the left holding only clutter. The stairs leading up to the residence above are against the northeast wall with a pile of firewood and some more food barrels underneath.

Riverwood Trader upstairs

Upstairs there are two owned single beds in the southern and western corners, with a dresser and round wooden table between them. On the dresser are three common books and on the table are two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a common book and three loose gold coins. At the foot of both beds are novice-locked chests containing minor loot. In the center of the room is a long wooden table with three bottles of alto wine, several loaves of bread, and pieces of cheese. Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and more clutter. In the northern corner, over the stairs, are a couple of unusable barrels and a square wooden table, with a door leading outside onto a balcony overlooking the main road through town.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Respawning "Skyrim:Dungeons") after ten days.

- 1 [Iron Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet")
- 3 [Iron Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow")
- 2 [Wooden Bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Bowl "Skyrim:Wooden Bowl")
- 4 [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), 2 [Bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), 1 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), 3 [Eidar Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), 4 [Goat Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), 6 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), 3 [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine")
- 2 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire")
- 1 [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), 1 [Iron Mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), 1 [Iron Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), 1 [Steel Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword")

## Notes

- All low-value items in the store can be freely taken once you have completed [The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw") quest.
- Before The Golden Claw is completed, the Riverwood Trader will remain open all day, every day, and Camilla and Lucan will never leave the store or sleep.
- After the Golden Claw is returned to Lucan and Camilla, it is displayed on the counter but is never for sale - not even with the "Merchant" perk. If you want it back again (for instance to display in one of your properties), you will have to steal it.
- If you place items in the cupboard behind Lucan's counter, they will show up in his inventory. Purchasing stolen items you place in there will remove their stolen tags. Don't put torches in there, though, as they won't add to what Lucan has for sale.
- Multiple internal references to this location bear the name "Lucan's Dry Goods", which is also the name that still gets displayed on your local map in the final game.
  - The store's related investor list bears the internal name of `PerkInvestorRiverwoodWhiteriverTraderList`, implying that "Whiteriver Trader" or "White River Trader" might've also once been an early name.

## Bugs

- It is possible to invest in the Riverwood Trader so that the merchant's available cash can be permanently increased to up to 10750 gold.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- Even if you finish The Golden Claw, the items in the chest next to the dresser on the first floor may still need to be stolen. **?**

Riverwood

**Riverwood** is a lumber milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in southern [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").

Nestled between the western slopes of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), and the banks of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), Riverwood lies just beyond the northern border of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). Three roads lead into it from the east, north and south, making it an easy access point from other holds. It's the town closest to where you start the game and has some basic facilities available, including a sawmill where you can earn money, a blacksmith, a general goods store in the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader"), and a tavern and inn named the [Sleeping Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn").

Riverwood is a good town in which to start off your character. With the options and work available, you can quickly learn many of the game's crafting features, encounter quest-giving NPCs, and earn a decent amount of coin in a short amount of time.

#### Side Quests

- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").

#### Main Quest

- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

## Notes

- The initial conversation scene between [Hilde](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilde "Skyrim:Hilde") and [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven") beginning with "A dragon! I saw a dragon!" only takes place before 8pm, 17th of Last Seed, 4E201.
- Across the river, directly west of the mill, is the treasure chest for [Treasure Map I](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_I "Skyrim:Treasure Map I"), assuming you have the map.
- Near the main bridge north of town is a salmon rack. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, there will also be a fishing rod and a copy of *[Line and Lure](/wiki/Skyrim:Line_and_Lure "Skyrim:Line and Lure")* leaning against some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies").
- After completing [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), there is a 20% chance of [encountering](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") a [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Thief (Thieves Guild)") trying to break into Riverwood Trader.
- Across the main bridge to Riverwood, a duplicated bird sound effect appears to be placed in one spot near a tree. On closer inspection, you'll find four red-winged blackbird models stacked on top of each other stuck inside the tree.
- According to *[The Art of Skyrim](/wiki/Books:The_Art_of_Skyrim "Books:The Art of Skyrim")*, Riverwood was the prototype for the towns in the game, and was the first area to be fully developed.
- Riverwood also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Riverwood "Arena:Riverwood") in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*.

## Bugs

- Upon arriving in Riverwood with [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") at the start of a new game, [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") may be dead somewhere in town for no apparent reason. If this is the case, the quest [A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") cannot be started, and subsequently neither Faendal nor Sven can be recruited as followers.
- Residents are sometimes seen walking through the river water instead of using a closer path.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If the Stormcloaks take Whiterun Hold, the Whiterun Guards in Riverwood may not be replaced by Stormcloak Soldiers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Riverwood is extremely prone to [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attacks. The corpses of these dragons have trouble "cleaning up properly", and remain in the town for excessive amounts of time. This results in bones clipping through buildings and performance drops.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- If you commit a crime in Riverwood, leave the town for over 24 in-game hours, then return, the guards will not arrest you. All of the townspeople will be hostile toward you, although killing them will not yield a higher bounty, and the guards will not attack you. Fast traveling to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and paying off the bounty or going to jail will fix the glitch.

## Gallery

- 

  Protective wall
- 

  Fishing supplies in Riverwood

# Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the item, see [Rjorn's Drum (item)](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum_(item) "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum (item)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane") |
| Location(s): | [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"), [Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn") |
| Reward: | +1 to all [Combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") skills |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane")) |
| ID: | BardsCollegeDrum |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") | | |

What happened in [Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn")?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").
2. Travel to [Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn").
3. Retrieve [Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum_(item) "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum (item)").
4. Return to Giraud Gemane.

### The Dean of History

Once you have completed the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") initiation quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), the Dean of History, [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane"), will start saying: *"They found it! They actually found it!"* When asked what 'they' found, he will explain: *"Rjorn's drum! Nobody knows where he died, and therefore where his drum might be. Halldir was the missing link. Rjorn entered Halldir's Cairn in secret, and presumably died there. Now all I need to do is find someone to get it. Wait. You. You could do it. I need you to get me that drum."* He then proceeds to explain why the drum is worth going through the trouble, as Rjorn was the most famous battle drummer of the second age and the drum itself was used at half a dozen famous battles. He finishes with: *"Rjorn was always looking for new stories to tell. It seems he was writing a lay about Halldir when he vanished. That was the missing clue."* Although the task sounds quite dangerous, Giraud will then resume to his usual routine while it is up to you to track down the drum.

### Halldir's Cairn

Three dead bodies and a beam of energy

[Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn") is a cave, located a small ways southwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). Upon entering, it becomes obvious that something is very wrong in the cave, as you will find the bodies of three dead bandits, [Agrius](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrius "Skyrim:Agrius"), [Vidgrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidgrod "Skyrim:Vidgrod"), and [Raen](/wiki/Skyrim:Raen "Skyrim:Raen"). The three bodies lie around a huge beam of blue light that shoots into a hole in the ceiling, and the various skeletal remains suggest that the position of the dead bandits are not coincidental. Nearby are the three bed rolls, while a pedestal conveniently holds the [key to Halldir's crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Halldir%27s_Crypt "Skyrim:Key to Halldir's Crypt") along with a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Agrius's Journal") written by Agrius, detailing the last days of the three bandits:

***"Never thought I'd see the day we were run out of the [Knifepoint Gang](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge"). Least the storm should cover our tracks. Vidgrod, Raen, and I took shelter in a cave for the night. Looks like there's an old ruin here. Least there are no Draugr around."***

Unlock the iron door to the southwest and head up the spiral staircase. Pick up the various [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") along the way and head west at the intersection. As you approach the wooden door, two [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Ghost "Skyrim:Undead") will attack you, so dispose of them and unlock the door.

### Tombs of the Undead

You will enter some catacombs, with another ghost getting up from a throne as you approach. Head up the western set of stairs, past the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), to another tomb, where [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies will start to rise from their graves, along with more ghosts. A pedestal holds a useful copy of the spell tome [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie"), while the handle to raise the iron bars is found behind the throne.

***"Something's wrong. Raen hasn't said a word since she woke up this morning, just keeps staring off into space. Vidgrod isn't much better. They sick? Not like any illness I ever heard of. I'd just walk out on them, but I can't seem to get up the nerve. I feel like something's holding me back. What is this place?"***

The next chamber contains a puzzle with [rune totems](/wiki/Skyrim:Rune_Totems "Skyrim:Rune Totems") so clear the area of undead and consider picking the lock on the door to the southeast for a locked chest with minor loot. The puzzle is quite simple; the rotating symbols can be found on the pillar in the center of the chamber and need to match the symbols on the wall opposite them. Once all three are positioned correctly, pull the lever and watch the stone wall to the north disappear. Two more ghosts await in the next area and, while you can proceed up the stairs to the north, the western path has a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggering a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from the ceiling. At the dead end is a chest set up with a [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that will release the [flamethrower statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues"), so approach with caution. Take the stairs to the north until you reach your final destination, the chamber of Halldir:

### Halldir

***"We're not alone. I can hear him now. Someone, speaking in my mind. Old. Powerful. Halldir, that's the name. He wants something from us. Needs us to stay for the magic to work. I tried to run, can't. Just like them."***

The powerful draugr, Halldir

The chamber is where the blue beam of light ends and as you approach, a powerful draugr, [Halldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir "Skyrim:Halldir"), will be immersed in it. He is a leveled draugr caster with several [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells. He'll begin to speak in an ancient [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") tongue as you start to take away his health. At about 66% health, he will disappear and split into three different elemental versions of himself. All three are casters and are spread out enough to make this part rather difficult; as such, [magic resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") is recommended. The cold and fire casters are close to the room's entrance, while the lightning version sits apart. Focus on taking out the fire one first as his fire spells will cause massive burst damage. The cold one should be next, as he can severely reduce your movement speed. Finally, take out the lightning version of Halldir, and his ghost should materialize in the very center of the blue beam, obviously living off the souls of the three dead bandits below and before them, Rjorn. His ghost is not particularly powerful but carries the unique [Halldir's Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Staff "Skyrim:Halldir's Staff") with a [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") enchantment, so dispose of the draugr quickly. After the battle, the blue beam of light will disappear and everything goes quiet. You will now have free access to the boss chest, where [Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum_(item) "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum (item)") is hidden, along with a huge amount of valuable loot. Lastly, open the trap door in the middle and follow in the footsteps of Agrius, Vidgrod, and Raen - and legendary battle drummer Rjorn:

***"Raen jumped first. Onto the cairn. That's what Master wants - blood, sacrifice, power to live again. His magic, I can feel it pulsing in my blood. He's draining us. We'll serve him soon, our bodies, our souls. Just like the others. They're waiting. It's my turn."***

### Return with the Drum

Return to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and find Giraud Gemane. When you show him the drum he will be overwhelmed with joy: *"At last! I have searched for this drum for 20 years. The college treasury is a bit thin right now. But I can show you some tricks I learned from my days with the army."* He will then raise all your [Combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") skills by one point in return. This includes [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"), and [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed").

## Notes

- It is possible to sneak in slowly and kill Halldir using a sufficiently powerful bow attack just as the draugr-form appears. This will bypass the fight with Halldir and his clones.

## Bugs

- After you turn in the quest, the drum will remain in your inventory, still marked as a quest item.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- If Giraud Gemane dies before receiving the drum, it will remain in your inventory as a quest item. **?**
  - The drum can be removed from your inventory with the console command `player.removeitem daba9 1`.
- If you find the drum before activating the quest, it will not be marked as completed even after returning the drum.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  - On PC, you can prevent this by typing `SetStage BardsCollegeDrum 40` before returning the drum.
- After killing Halldir, if he dropped his staff, you can get two copies by looting his remains and picking it up off the floor (either order).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The pillars for the rune totem puzzle may not move when activated. **?**
- In Skyrim Special Edition, instead of splitting himself into three clones, Halldir sometimes just disappears. The player is left locked in the room with the drum but no staff and no way of opening the exit. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Give Rjorn's Drum to Giraud |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BardsCollegeDrum stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BardsCollegeDrum`.

# Skyrim:Roadside Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Dwelling.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Dwelling.png) | Nordic Dwelling: Roadside Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Roadside+Ruins)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")* | |

| Location | |
| Northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") | |

Roadside Ruins

**Roadside Ruins** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan").

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.

## Walkthrough

The site is an overgrown stone dome-shaped structure formed by two concentric circles. A spriggan is wandering in the innermost circle. Climbing to the top of the ruin offers an elevated view and easy access to the center and the spriggan. The corpses of two [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") are at the entrance to the outer circle on the southeast side, and two samples of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") grow in the outer circle. Windows around the perimeter of the inner wall offer a view of the overgrown atrium in the center and an opportunity for a ranged attack on the spriggan. The entry to the inner circle is on the north side of the inner wall. Despite the abundant flora, the only alchemically useful specimens in the inner circle are three [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") plants and five samples of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"). A chest is directly opposite the inner entrance on the southeast wall, with a copy of the [Enchantment](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")* propped against the front of the chest.

With the [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, an altar will be added with three bowls labeled "Fortune", "Power", and "Nothing". You may choose to fill one of these bowls during the quest [A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish").

# Skyrim:Robber's Gorge (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find the [treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge#Bandit_Chief_Treasure "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") of [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") |
| Reward: | Leveled Treasure |
| ID: | dunRobbersGorgeQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

Ambush at [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge")

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Investigate [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") for a secret trapdoor.
2. Find the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Bandit Leader's Journal") in [Robber's Cove](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge#Robber.27s_Cove "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge").
3. Follow the clues to the bandit leader's secret treasure.

### Ambush

The camp near [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River")

On the road between [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), near [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") has taken over an old overhanging bridge and set up a clever method for ambushing travelers and caravans. As soon as you approach the bridge, the bandits will release a few [boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") to block the path, then talk to you from their safe spot above: *"All right, that's far enough. You know how this works- toll here is 100 gold."* If you question the meaning of a "toll" in the middle of nowhere, you will be told: *"Don't play dumb with me. Pay up, and you walk right through. Refuse, and you'll never see the other side."* You can choose to pay the gold and they will let you pass unharmed, while the other options will make them turn hostile. Regardless of your choice, the bandit camp at [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") has been set up right next to the road, so head up there and the bandits will attack anyway. Kill the bandit guarding the entrance and deal with the three on the overhanging bridge, then enter Robber's Gorge through the door.

### Robber's Gorge

A cave with a clue

The huge camp is an extension of the ambush bridge and consists of several tents with bedrolls. A few bandits will attack you on sight as you enter. Your target is the wooden house in the southern section of the camp: the home of the Bandit Leader. He will attack the moment you enter, so defeat him and take a look around for the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill book *[The Black Arrow, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arrow,_v2 "Skyrim:The Black Arrow, v2")* on a table and a chest with some decent loot. The bandit leader carries a boss-leveled amount of gold along with the [key to Robber's Cove](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Robber%27s_Cove "Skyrim:Key to Robber's Cove"). Alternatively, a second key can be found on a dresser in one of the bedrooms. Claim the key and locate the trap door leading underground to the hidden cave, [Robbers' Cove](/wiki/Skyrim:Robbers%27_Cove "Skyrim:Robbers' Cove").

### A Paranoid Bandit Leader

The island to the south

The cove turns out to be a secret sanctuary for the bandit leader and is merely a small ledge and an underground lake filled with [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"). Some food is present along with a docked boat, some weaponry, and an empty chest (this chest will contain the quest item if you are on one of the related quests). If you jump in the water, some more minor treasure can be found as well as several skeletons. Investigate the table and read through the *[Bandit Leader's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Bandit Leader's Journal")*. The pages reveal his worries about his relationship with his men and his fears about an upcoming mutiny. He apparently started to take some of the gold earned from the ambushes, a little bit of a time, and was waiting to gather enough gold to escape to Dragon Bridge. Lastly, after one of his companions unexpectedly visited the cove, the bandit leader decided to move his stash to a better location:

***"I don't think he found my stash, but it's not safe here. I took the boat out tonight and stowed it on the island to the south, by the old tree stump."***

Jump into the water and leave the cove through the southern exit. Keep swimming south and you will immediately see a waterfall. At the foot of the waterfall is the island described in the journal, including the old tree stump. Next to the stump is the bandit leader's stash hidden away in a chest, so use the key to unlock it and claim his ill-gotten gains for yourself.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 11, 20, 30, 40, 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunRobbersGorgeQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunRobbersGorgeQST`.

# Skyrim:Robber's Gorge

## Overview

Robber's Gorge

**Robber's Gorge** is a small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave west-southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). It contains only one zone, *[Robbers' Cove](#Robbers.27_Cove)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge_(quest) "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge (quest)")**: Find the [treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge#Bandit_Chief_Treasure "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") of Robber's Gorge.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The camp is along the road from [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") to [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") just north of [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal"), with an overpass bridge controlled by the bandits spanning the road. While the main entrance to the camp is the gate along the road, a covert approach from the southwest will permit you to snipe the guard sentries controlling the trap levers from the bridge.

Seven bandits guard the area: two archers are on the bridge, one bandit guards the western gate, one bandit guards the northern rear entrance, and the remaining three bandits are within the camp's wooden palisade. The Bandit Chief is inside the house. Three [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") are at the western entrance, while three [falling boulder traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") along the road are triggered by levers (one on the west side of the bridge and two on the east) at the lookout towers above.

The Bandit Chief carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Robber%27s_Cove "Skyrim:Key to Robber's Cove") that unlocks two [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in *Robbers' Cove*. Inside the house is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arrow, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arrow,_v2 "Skyrim:The Black Arrow, v2")* on the table, another key, leveled loot, and a bedroll in the eastern room.

### Robbers' Cove

There are no enemies in this area. The *[Bandit Leader's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Bandit Leader's Journal")* is on the table. The treasure chest to the left is expert-locked but can be unlocked with the key found outside; it will be open and empty if you are not on a related quest. To the right, a skeletal hand can be seen floating on the surface of the water. Below it lies the rest of the skeleton and a coin purse. In the northeastern corner of the cove, an adept-locked chest sits underwater next to armor and weapons. Six [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), five [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), five [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and one [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") can be found in the cove.

The journal recounts the chief bandit's mutinous strife with his crew and his plans to stash away gold, indicating he eventually accrued enough to run away before being murdered by his own crew. The journal notes he hid his stash by a tree stump on the island to the south. Exit the cove and head directly south toward the waterfall, where the chest is on the south side of the tree stump. The chest is master-locked but can be unlocked with the key.

## Notes

- The bandits may stop you and demand that you pay a toll of 100 gold.
- To leave the water without exiting the cove, swim up against the boat and jump. This will get you onto the low rocks beside the dock. The only other way out of the water takes you out of the cove, so it is advisable to leave submerged loot until the rest of the loot in the cove has been collected if you have trouble with the boat trick.

## Bugs

- The cove's interior cell has the apostrophe after the "s" (*Robbers' Cove*), whereas the map name, related bandit faction, and the location's key use "Robber's".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, addresses this issue. The interior cell has been renamed to *Robber's Cove*.
- The main water plane in the Cove is filled with holes, allowing you to slip through at the borders.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |

| [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 4 |

Rockwallow Mine

**Rockwallow Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in eastern [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"). It contains only one zone, *[Rockwallow Mine](#Rockwallow_Mine)*.

It is owned by Thane [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and run by the married couple [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur") and [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder"). [Gestur Rockbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Gestur_Rockbreaker "Skyrim:Gestur Rockbreaker") will [buy iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Rockwallow Mine Camp |
| --- |
| [Gestur Rockbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Gestur_Rockbreaker "Skyrim:Gestur Rockbreaker")  [Hjaalmarch Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Guard "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Guard")  [Jesper](/wiki/Skyrim:Jesper "Skyrim:Jesper")  [Swanhvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Swanhvir "Skyrim:Swanhvir")  [Teeba-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Teeba-Ei "Skyrim:Teeba-Ei") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery")**: Tell [Thane Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") that the late shipment from Rockwallow Mine will be arriving soon.

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is outside the mine entrance, which is east of [Sorli's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli%27s_House "Skyrim:Sorli's House").

### Rockwallow Mine

The entrance is a short, ice-filled tunnel leading to a central icy cave containing two wooden ramps up to platforms each within reach of an iron ore vein: one directly in front of you (to the east) and the other on your right (in the southwest). The latter has a bedroll beside a low table holding a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")*. In the northeast and southeast, two short tunnels lead to dead ends, each with an iron ore vein at the end. Several [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and shovels are found throughout the mine.

## Notes

- During the day, there are as many miners as ore veins, making it difficult to mine.

# Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Deliver a letter to a [farmer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Rogatus Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") |
| Location(s): | [Salvius Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Salvius Farmhouse"), [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn") |
| Reward: | 25 [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Rogatus Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius")) |
| ID: | FreeformSalviusFarmA |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Leontius, the Prodigal Son

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Rogatus Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") at [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm").
2. Agree to take a letter to his son.
3. Deliver [Rogatus's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter_(item) "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter (item)") to [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius") at [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn").

### Just Another Day on the Farm

Salvius Farmhouse is just to the east of [Markarth Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Stables "Skyrim:Markarth Stables") as you approach [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The farm is tended by Rogatus Salvius and his wife [Vigdis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigdis_Salvius "Skyrim:Vigdis Salvius"), and Salvius will be outside during most of the daylight hours. Speaking to him will reveal a caustic nature and a long list of complaints. At the moment, he is upset at his son who works at the Old Hroldan Inn and never visits. He'll ask you to do him a favor by delivering a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter_(item) "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter (item)") admonishing his son for his familial neglect.

### Some Things Never Change

Old Hroldan Inn is across the hold, almost directly east of Markarth. Traveling along the road will take you near a few [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") encampments, but should be relatively safe. It can also be approached by traveling over the mountains to the west of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Leontius Salvius is typically outside chopping wood or on the porch during the day. He can be found inside the inn at night. He'll thank you for the letter, wistfully reproaching the content, and pay you twenty-five gold for delivering the letter.

## Notes

- This quest is nearly identical to [Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery") radiant quests, but is not included in their radiant scheme.

## Bugs

- Rogatus may not have any dialogue when you try to return his letter.
  - Try the usual methods, such as restarting, resetting, cache clearing, and resting. Coming back after doing other things may work as well.
- If pickpocketed back from Leontius, the letter will still be marked as a quest item and can't be dropped.
  - Typing `player.removeitem 000931c2 1` into the console will remove it from the player's inventory.

## Quest Stages

| Rogatus's Letter (FreeformSalviusFarmA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Deliver Rogatus's letter to Leonitus *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformSalviusFarmA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformSalviusFarmA`.

## Overview

Romlyn Dreth's House

**Romlyn Dreth's House** is a dwelling in the lower part of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), by the canal that runs through the city.

It is found next to the stairs leading down to the canal from in front of [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth") |

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Romlyn Dreth's House

Romlyn Dreth at home

Just to the left of the entrance are two [fish barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") that you are free to take from. It is a single room dwelling, like all the homes all the canal-side with a partial wall separating the living and sleeping quarters. Upon entering you are in the living area that consists of a fireplace in the middle of the west wall, with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two bunches of [frost mirraim](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging above. Located in the northwest corner is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") and a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"). Situated in front of the fireplace are three chairs and a round wooden table holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). There is a dresser holding [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") against the partial east wall and hanging above it are three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two garlic braids and a bunch of elves ear. There are a set of shelves and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the south wall. The shelves are holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several pieces of cheese. Barrels and sacks containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") are situated all around this room as well.

The sleeping area consists of a single owned bed in the northwest corner, with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") under it and on the west wall a wall shelf over the bed. On the shelf is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Further along the west wall by the foot of the bed is an end table holding a wooden bowl containing [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and to the right of the bed against the south wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door.

Rorik's Manor

**Rorik's Manor** is the small home of [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik"), the head of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and his best friend and companion [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette").

While the name suggests that it would be a grand house, Rorik's Manor is not much bigger than the other farmhouses in Rorikstead, which he owns. It is a single-story L-shaped building located at the northwestern end of the village.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik")  [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette") |

### Exterior

The only items of interest are a campfire with an empty pot hanging over it and an unowned bedroll beside it. There are two [cows](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") in an animal pen to the east of the house.

### Rorik's Manor

The fireplace is opposite the entrance and has a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of it and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the mantelpiece. The western end of the house is filled with several bales of straw, barrels and a large pile of firewood. To the right of the fireplace, against the north wall is a long wooden table and a kettle containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). On the table are two more potatoes, a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"). Above the table are two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and two garlic braids. To the right of these is a rack hanging from the ceiling which holds two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

To the right of the table is a flower basket containing four more chicken's eggs. Further along the north wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and three of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). In the northeast corner is a dresser containing a selection of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and two [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") on top. Beside this, coming out from the east wall is a single owned bed, where [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette") sleeps. There is an end table beside the bed and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot beside that.

A counter coming out from the east wall to the right of all this with several sacks and a barrel, all containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around it. On the counter are several bottles of wine, alto wine and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") along with several pieces of cheese. Under the counter is a copy of *[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")* and an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"). There is a chair and [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") behind the counter and a wardrobe further to the right of that. Coming out from the south wall is a large double bed that [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik") uses with an end table on either side. On the left-hand end table is a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling") and beside it on the floor is a medium coin purse. The right-hand end table has four loose septims on top. To the right of the bed against the west wall are a couple of barrels with more bottles of wine and alto wine on them, while further right is a small round wooden table and two chairs. On this table is a couple of bottles of Nord mead.

# Skyrim:Rorikstead

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 2 |

Rorikstead

**Rorikstead** is a farming [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in western [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").

The town is named after the noble [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik"), who owns a local "[manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik%27s_Manor "Skyrim:Rorik's Manor")". Despite its living namesake, Rorikstead is mentioned in two much older accounts: The [Merethic](/wiki/Lore:Merethic_Era "Lore:Merethic Era") or [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era") text *[Holdings of Jarl Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Holdings_of_Jarl_Gjalund "Skyrim:Holdings of Jarl Gjalund")* (as "Rorik's Steading") and the [Second Era](/wiki/Lore:Second_Era "Lore:Second Era") text *[Atlas of Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Atlas_of_Dragons "Skyrim:Atlas of Dragons")*. It is also mentioned in the bard's song *[Ragnar the Red](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Songs of Skyrim")* as "ole Rorikstead", which may indicate the current town is named after an ancient predecessor. The town contains several crop fields, and the residents claim not to have had a bad harvest in years.

## Rorikstead Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

#### Daedric

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

#### Side Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.

## Notes

- With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, you can use the grain mills here to make [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour").
- Atop the hill north of the town is a [shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") featuring a [dragon scale](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Scales "Skyrim:Dragon Scales") and a copy of the book *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*. This is the only place where you can obtain a dragon scale prior to completing the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising").
- After the quest Dragon Rising, you are likely to encounter a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attacking Rorikstead. Fittingly, [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") will [mention](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dialogue#Town-Specific "Skyrim:Guard Dialogue") how Rorikstead is usually a calm place but is vulnerable to a dragon attack. Throughout most of the game, this encounter is likely to be with a random unnamed dragon; however, the named dragon [Nahagliiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahagliiv "Skyrim:Nahagliiv") is buried in a [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds#Rorikstead_Resurrection "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") not far west of the town and will be resurrected by [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") during the quest [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall").[*verification needed — Do the game mechanics have a special heightened ratio of dragon attacks for Rorikstead?*]
- [Lokir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lokir "Skyrim:Lokir"), one of the NPCs in the carriage during the quest [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), states he is from Rorikstead, but he has no residence and is not mentioned by anyone in town.

## Bugs

- None of the livestock animals here are owned, allowing you to kill them without any crime penalties at all.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9, fixes this bug.

## Quick Walkthrough

Find the Fishing Supplies in the assigned city. Use them and start fishing. When the line pulls strong without water splashing, you have an item hooked. Keep doing this until you have all four.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Go to the mentioned area and fish for rubbish. It works better with the standard fishing rod.

## Bugs

- Due to an issue with how the fishing supply objects were set up, it is unlikely you'll ever get this quest in Dawnstar or Morthal.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Radiant_3 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Radiant_3`.

# Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft

## Overview

Ruins of Bthalft

The **Ruins of Bthalft** are a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

The hidden entrance to the [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") can be found here.

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Fan Favorite](/wiki/Skyrim:Fan_Favorite "Skyrim:Fan Favorite")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dwarven_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dwarven Mail"): Track down a fugitive Arena combatant.
- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The entrance to the Aetherium Forge

This location is used by three (two without [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed) bandits as their camp. Due to the ruin's proximity to [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp"), the bandits and soldiers often engage each other. There are arches at the northern and southern ends of the camp with hanging [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"). Between the arches is a stone-floored area with several crates, barrels, and sacks. A third arch to the southeast leads up to the statue containing the machinery to gain access to the Aetherium Forge. Near the northern end are wooden stairs leading up to an adept-locked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), some crates, a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack. A [Dwemer Convector](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Convector "Skyrim:Dwemer Convector"), used for [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"), is behind the wall to the north between the two arches.

With Dawnguard installed, a tower can be raised after finding all four [Aetherium Shards](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard") during [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages"). It gives access to the Aetherium Forge.

## Notes

- One [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein is east of the circular area.
- Without Dawnguard installed, some hanging [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids and [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") can be harvested here.

## Bugs

- Although the bandits aren't supposed to respawn at this location after Dawnguard is installed, the bandits can still respawn even with the add-on.
- Due to a rare inventory reference corruption bug, it may be possible to attempt to place an Aetherium Shard on the pedestal here with the Dawnguard add-on and have the pedestal instead remove a different item from your inventory. As a result, Lost to the Ages will then become stuck and you will be unable to open the entry into the Aetherium Forge. The removed item is permanently lost, and the shards are then permanently stuck in your inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. The DLC1LD\_AetheriumPedestal script has been altered to deal directly with the MiscObject base forms instead of using alias reference checks. This allows the quest to continue on with proper activation of the pedestal and removal of the actual Aetherium Shards. This ISN'T a fix the underlying inventory reference bug that caused this. It is only a workaround to prevent this quest from getting blocked by it.


---

# Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Ruins of Rkund ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother"), [Wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RkundExterior01 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") Southeast of [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") | |

Ruins of Rkund

The **Ruins of Rkund** are a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in the mountains southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother") and [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp").

## Walkthrough

The ruins are most easily accessed by passing through the [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven")-infested [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") and heading southeast into the mountains. They consist of a few broken pillars and collapsed buildings; the one farthest to the east contains an unlocked [Dwemer chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). In front of this is a Dwemer floor lantern in a stone pit, with the bodies of two [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") lying next to it, along with a few pieces of [Dwemer metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Metal "Skyrim:Dwemer Metal") and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). As you approach the ruins, three [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp") will be seen roaming the area. Approaching the lantern will trigger the appearance of their [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother"). The only other items of interest are a few [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes in the area.

## Bugs

- The two dead hags may appear with their clothing unequipped.
- The wisps don't seem to respawn.
- You may have to attack the lantern in the center in order to trigger the wispmother event.

# Skyrim:Runoff Caverns

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Runoff Caverns ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Runoff+Caverns+%28CC%29)) | | |

Runoff Caverns

**Runoff Caverns** is a large [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt") containing mercenaries, [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains seven zones: *[Runoff Caverns](#Runoff_Caverns)*, *[Vardnknd Gallery](#Vardnknd_Gallery)*, *[Autumn's Bells](#Autumn.27s_Bells)*, *[Spring's Symphony](#Spring.27s_Symphony)*, *[Summer's Chords](#Summer.27s_Chords)*, *[Winter's Chimes](#Winter.27s_Chimes)*, and *[Vardnknd Skykiller Gallery](#Vardnknd_Skykiller_Gallery)*.

The caverns hold the ruins of **Vardnknd**, which houses a dangerous Dwemer "weather witch" device capable of manipulating the weather across all of Skyrim. Several zones within the caverns feature distinct climates and related environments.

## Related Quests

- **[Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Shut down a malfunctioning Dwarven weather machine.
- **[The Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Reassemble an ancient Dwarven [vamidium](/wiki/Lore:Vamidium "Lore:Vamidium").
- **[The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Gather all the components of a powerful Dwarven Crown from within a forgotten Dwarven ruin.

### Exterior

The exterior appears to be an unassuming cave entrance, distinguished only by the strange torso of a Broken Dwarven Horse found sitting in a pool of water nearby. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") nearby. As it is found high up in the mountains, it can be most easily reached by going southwest past [Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower").

### Runoff Caverns

The entrance to Vardnknd

This section of the dungeon transitions from a natural cavern to a Dwarven ruin. You will need to descend to the bottom of the main chamber and explore the side passages in order to access the ruins of Vardnknd. The central drawbridge can be lowered from the other side of the main chamber after navigating all the way around the chamber, creating a shortcut back to the entrance. This section is filled with hostile mercenaries and Dwarven automatons.

### Vardnknd Gallery

Vardnknd Gallery machinery

This section functions as a hub area for the entire dungeon, connecting to each of the other sections. [Elberon](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon "Skyrim:Elberon") can be found here, and will be struck by lightning the minute you enter *Vardnknd Gallery*. [Elberon's Apprentice](/wiki/Skyrim:Elberon%27s_Apprentice "Skyrim:Elberon's Apprentice") will spawn here as part of the quest [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)").

Each of the four seasonal rooms accessed from this section has an area outside the door where the climate within has begun to spread into the main chamber. The scenery hints at what season you will be entering. The climatic extremes allow the vegetation in Spring and Autumn to grow gigantic, and for populations of herbivorous animals to spend their whole lives in these ecosystems.

Each seasonal room has previously been explored by mercenaries in Elberon's employ; none of them have survived long enough to meet you, but one in each section (the first corpse encountered) will carry a note in their inventory explaining how to navigate the room and the tasks needed to obtain the conduit gem.

### Autumn's Bells

Autumn's Bells

The door to this section is the northwest of the four season doors. Just outside it, an autumnal harvest of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), cabbage, [wild spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Wild Spiky Grass"), and wild gourds grows. Unlootable humanoid bones lie half-hidden in the vegetation.

This section consists of a large Dwarven chamber filled with wild spiky grass and fields of strange glowing wheat being maintained by hostile Dwarven automatons. The [Dwarven Autumn Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Autumn_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Autumn Visage") and all parts for the quest [The Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse") can be found here. The chamber also contains its own wildlife, including many strangely colored [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit").

### Spring's Symphony

Spring's Symphony

The entrance to this section is the southeast of the four season doors. Just outside the door, birdsong is heard and giant mountain flowers of all types grow gigantic in a small meadow. Of note are incredibly rare, unplantable [yellow mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Yellow Mountain Flower") which can otherwise only be found in locations added by the Dawnguard add-on (such as Ancestor Glade).

This section consists of winding Dwarven passages filled with a green haze. The path is blocked by roots at several points, and can only be unblocked by killing a nearby [Blooming Spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Blooming_Spriggan "Skyrim:Blooming Spriggan"). This section is filled with various hostile and passive animals and also contains a boss-level [Blooming Spriggan Matron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blooming_Spriggan_Matron "Skyrim:Blooming Spriggan Matron"). The [Dwarven Spring Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spring_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Spring Visage") and [Dwarven Drone Fly](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Drone_Fly "Skyrim:Dwarven Drone Fly") can be found here.

### Summer's Chords

Summer's Chords

The entrance to this room is the northeastern door, just past Elberon's campsite. The doorway is on a landing where two sets of stairs on either side meet. Rather fittingly, it is next to the main room's lava pool.

This section is made up of lava-filled chambers crossed by various bridges and pipes. It contains hostile [flame atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") and automatons, as well as several [flame-spraying pipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Traps") that stop and go at regular intervals. As explained by the *[Note on Summer](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_Summer "Skyrim:Note on Summer")*, you will need to guide a [Repair Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Repair_Spider "Skyrim:Repair Spider") through this zone to activate each service waypoint dotted throughout; a [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod_(Forgotten_Seasons) "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod (Forgotten Seasons)") can be found near the entrance for this purpose. Disabling the waypoints at the far end of each room is also important.

The spider itself is spawned by flipping a lever near where the rod is found; the dead mercenary who carries the *Note on Summer* is also found here, presumably having succumbed to the heat before being able to release the spider. The narrow walkways combined with having one or more followers may temporarily impede the spider's movement past you to the next service waypoint, but it may visually "teleport" to the spot you have indicated and be able to disable the waypoint.

There are only two chests in this room. All other loot is recovered from enemies in the area.

### Winter's Chimes

Winter's Chimes

The entrance to this section is through the southwest door. Just outside this door, a snowdrift has overflowed beneath the threshold and brings cold air with it into the main chamber. Several unlootable dead Automatons lie half-buried in this avalanche.

This section initially appears to be a snowy exterior area, but is in fact a large natural cavern which is subject to unending, artificially chilly weather. It is filled with vertical Dwarven architecture and half-frozen pools of water. You must be willing to jump down several long drops into deep pools of water; presumably this is why followers cannot accompany you here. Although merely a visual effect in the base game, the cold winds and icy waters of this section are compatible with the [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") Creation and will be a severe challenge to navigate if you are playing with it enabled due to its effect on your character's [Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold "Skyrim:Cold") attribute. This area is filled with [Frosted Dwarven Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frosted_Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Frosted Dwarven Spider"), [frost atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Frost Atronach"), and ice wraiths, and contains a boss-level [Frosted Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Frosted_Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Frosted Dwarven Centurion"). The [Dwarven Winter Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Winter_Visage "Skyrim:Dwarven Winter Visage") can be found here.

Note: There is a gap between platforms on the edge of one of the deep "wells" that can be crossed with 2 words of Whirlwind Sprint. Only one word is usually not enough, and all three words will cause you to overshoot the mark. However, traveling too far is not a big problem because you will be going in that direction anyway.

### Vardnknd Skykiller Gallery

This section is initially inaccessible and can only be accessed by means of a set of stairs in *[Vardnknd Gallery](#Vardnknd_Gallery)* which will rise as part of the quest Forgotten Seasons. It is one large chamber and contains the final boss of the dungeon, a giant Dwarven spider called [The Sky Orchestrator](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sky_Orchestrator "Skyrim:The Sky Orchestrator"), which will drop the [Ward of the Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward_of_the_Seasons "Skyrim:Ward of the Seasons") cuirass when defeated. You will then be able to claim the *[Turn of the Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_of_the_Seasons "Skyrim:Turn of the Seasons")* book and utilize a shortcut which will place you back at the beginning of *[Runoff Caverns](#Runoff_Caverns)*, near the exit.

## Notes

- This is the only location where wild spiky grass can be found.

## Bugs

- This location is marked as undiscovered on your map from the start of the game.
- The stairs leading to *Vardnknd Skykiller Gallery* may not rise visually, but you will still be able to ascend them once you've cleared all four of the seasonal zones.
- After finishing the quest and leaving the dungeon, if you return to *Vardnknd Gallery* then try to exit via *Vardnknd Skykiller Gallery*, the gate may be closed.
  -  From the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), use the `TCL` command to clip through the gate.
  - You can also just leave the long way around.

## Overview
