Rustleif's House

**Rustleif's House** is a smithy near [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar")'s shoreline. [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif") has his smithy and home set up facing the bay. He is a renowned weaponsmith, and he is often called upon to arm and outfit the jarl's men. His Redguard wife, [Seren](/wiki/Skyrim:Seren "Skyrim:Seren"), assists him and is pregnant. Both Rustleif and Seren provide merchant services.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")  [Seren](/wiki/Skyrim:Seren "Skyrim:Seren") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") |

### Exterior

Blacksmithing

There is a raised, covered porch in front and to the left of the door, with a couple of food barrels to the right and wooden benches to the left of the door. There are two sets of steps leading up to the porch and a snowberry bush beside one of them. On the side of the house the [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") setup is rather minimal, consisting of only a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and where they buy and sell their goods, although two [smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") can be found elsewhere in town. The front door is novice-locked during the day when they are both around the forge working and at night.

### Rustleif's House

Rustleif's house

The house is a single-room dwelling that is a little spartan inside. Upon entering, on your left is a long wooden table and bench holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). To the left of the table, on the floor is a basket containing four [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and to the right is a basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). Further to the right against the north wall is a set of shelves holding two leeks, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three potatoes, with several pieces of cheese on top. Above these shelves are two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling. There is a food barrel in the northeastern corner.

Against the east wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, beside a large double bed with a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") by the foot of it and a basket containing two [potions of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor") to the right and a round wooden table beside this holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). Next to this against the south wall is a tall wardrobe with a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") on top and pile of firewood, with a hang rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") between them. Opposite the door, on the south wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantlepiece. In front of the hearth is an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). To the right of the fireplace are several barrels and against the west wall is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") (unmatched, unenchanted; [Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") (unmatched, unenchanted; [Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (one of each type incl. [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") except [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"); unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) |  |
| 50 | [Iron Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") |  |
| 10 | [Iron Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") |  |
| 10 | Pieces of [Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") |  |

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Located overlooking the shoreline of Dawnstar, Rustleif has his smithy and home set up facing the main road. Rustleif is a renowned weaponsmith, and he is often called upon to arm and outfit the Jarl's men. His Redguard wife, Seren, assists him and is currently with child. Inside, their home is comfortable but a little spartan."*

# Skyrim:Ruunvald Excavation

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Ruunvald Excavation ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruunvald+Excavation+%28DG%29)) | | |

Ruunvald Excavation

**Ruunvald Excavation** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant") charmed by the conjurer [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne"). It contains two zones: *[Ruunvald Excavation](#Ruunvald_Excavation)* and *[Ruunvald Temple](#Ruunvald_Temple)*.

Before the start of the quest [Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks"), this location is named **Ruunvald Ruins**, and the entrances are key-locked and cannot be opened.

## Related Quests

- **[Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks")**: Find [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") and recruit him into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius")† |

† Relocates to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") after being rescued from here, only if you are joined to Dawnguard faction.

### Exterior

The excavation is high in the eastern mountains, south-southeast of [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave"). Beside the entrance is a large tent containing two unowned bedrolls, used by those on guard duty protecting the site from [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). The excavation was started by a team of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr") led by [Moric Sidrey](/wiki/Skyrim:Moric_Sidrey "Skyrim:Moric Sidrey"). Inside the tent by the bedrolls is a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe"), a pair of [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"), two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and *[Volk's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Volk%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Volk's Journal")*. The journal is by [Volk](/wiki/Skyrim:Volk "Skyrim:Volk"), who was one of the guards, and one of the last to enter the cave. In front of the tent is an old extinguished campfire and a banner hanging from a tall post. There is a lone [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush behind the tent, along with several crates and unusable barrels. The tent itself resembles the ones at [Imperial camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps#Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps"). The entrance consists of typical wooden doors seen on mines throughout [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). A lit lantern on a wooden post is to the left of the entrance.

### Ruunvald Excavation

Upon entering, you are in a supported tunnel descending to the north, leading down to a wooden ramp descending around the outside wall of a large chamber. Ahead is what appears to be one of the Vigilants of Stendarr, standing facing away from you at the entrance to another tunnel opposite. The ramp continues down past this tunnel to the ground below. It transpires that everyone within the site has been charmed and will attack you on sight; you are unable to even talk with them. To the right of the first [charmed Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Charmed_Vigilant "Skyrim:Charmed Vigilant") is a crate holding the journal *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. I")*, in which Moric documents the early progress of the expedition.

There is a second charmed Vigilant at the bottom of the chamber, who will also attack you on sight. There are numerous crates and barrels and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on and near a wooden platform at the bottom of the chamber. There is also an unowned bedroll and table on a second platform, with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") beside the bedroll. To the right of this platform is a [malachite ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Malachite Ore Vein").

The tunnel heads north and eventually opens into a wider tunnel, where several barrels, crates, and an empty cart are stored. There is a charmed Vigilant patrolling this part of the tunnel. The tunnel then descends further, passing another cart on your left containing three pieces of [malachite ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore "Skyrim:Malachite Ore"). Ahead is a junction where the tunnel turns southwest, but beware a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") across the passage. There is another charmed Vigilant on the right mining a malachite ore vein, and an alcove in front containing an unowned bedroll beside a table holding an empty [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Under the table is another loose coin, with a second burial urn to the right and an unlocked chest to the left. There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") on the ground, and an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above which is released by the tripwire. The tunnel continues to the southwest, passing several crates and barrels. On your right, on a crate is a [Scroll of Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Turn_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Turn Undead") and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

The tunnel turns left again, with a burial urn and an unlocked chest in front. Just after the turning, the tunnel opens into another large chamber, with a central rock pillar and plenty of wooden support beams. There is a charmed Vigilant mining a malachite ore vein below you. A ramp leads down on your right. At the bottom, there is a charmed Vigilant patrolling the chamber and a [husky](/wiki/Skyrim:Husky "Skyrim:Husky") farther back, who may be alerted by any fighting. To the right of the ore vein the Vigilant was mining is an open crate containing a piece of malachite ore. There are several pickaxes found around this chamber. On a wooden platform to the southwest is a bedroll, with a barrel and crates on either side. On these are a quiver of [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt"), a random [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), and two random [potions of healing, magicka, or stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Behind the central pillar is a lean-to with a bedroll under it and a crate beside it holding *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. II")*, which documents the success of the expedition, but also mentions losses of time and headaches.

To the east is another narrow tunnel that takes a couple of turns before entering a wider section partially floored with wood. In front is a short ramp down to a burial urn and an adept-locked chest. Beyond this first ramp and down a second ramp is an alcove on the right, with a charmed Vigilant sitting at a table with a medium coin purse on top and three unowned bedrolls beside it. There is also a husky in this alcove. The tunnel continues to the east before turning north once again, by a [fish barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Fish_Barrel "Skyrim:Containers") and a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). The turning leads to another wooden platform running around a chamber, with a ramp leading down to the right. There is a charmed Vigilant at the bottom, where you will find a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack and barrel under the ramp. To the south is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") beside a set of shelves holding ten [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), with a long wooden table in front holding *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. III")*. This journal is the first to mention [Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne "Skyrim:Minorne"), someone who seems to be constantly in Moric's thoughts. To the west, the tunnel is double width and filled with crates, barrels, and sacks, with a pillar of earth and rock supporting the ceiling. Take care, as there are a total of three [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") on the ground in this area. One is on either side of the pillar, triggering a single [crossbow bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolt "Skyrim:Bolt") from [mounted crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow_Mount "Skyrim:Crossbow Mount") on the ceiling and to the right, respectively. A third pressure plate where the tunnel narrows triggers two crossbow bolts from two mounted crossbows on barrels ahead. The three traps will only fire once each, and the four [crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") can all be taken. Past the pressure plates, the tunnel turns south, with a malachite ore vein in an alcove to the north.

The entrance to Ruunvald Temple

This next section begins to show signs of a Nordic barrow, and a large chamber ahead has a wooden bridge suspended from east to west. There is a charmed Vigilant wandering across the bridge, and many others nearby. Any fighting is likely to attract several of them, including Volk, the author of the journal found outside. On the western side of the bridge is a ramp leading down to the bottom of this chamber around the corner on your left, two empty open crates and an unowned bedroll on your right, and ahead at the back a small room containing an unlocked chest and a burial urn in the niche by the "window" overlooking the main room. In the corner by the ramp leading down is a square wooden table holding two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, as well as a small coin purse. The ramp descends to a walkway that is still above the ground connected to another suspended bridge that crosses the room from south to north, before another ramp leads down to the east. Ahead to the east is a cart filled with rocks and a piece of malachite ore; behind the cart is a skeleton crushed under a cave-in, with a pickaxe beside it. A tunnel leads farther down to the north on your left. Against the south wall to the right is a square table and chair, with a burial urn beside them. To the west is a brief descent to the lowest level of the chamber. Descending the tunnel to the north, the northeastern corner of the area features an alcove where Volk will be sitting at a table beside two food barrels and three sacks, if he was not previously alerted by fighting. The alcove also includes an owned single bed with an unlocked chest containing random loot at its foot, while on the table and one of the barrels are a small coin purse, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). Near the southwest corner of the area is a passage with distinctly Nordic architecture leading to doors to *[Ruunvald Temple](#Ruunvald_Temple)*. Just before this passage is *[Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Discovering_Ruunvald,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. IV")* on a barrel under the wooden structure supporting the previous walkways above.

### Ruunvald Temple

Through the door is a passage which staggers to the left after a short distance. At the corner is a carved stone head with an elk's skull and horns in front, candles on either side, and a book entitled *[Minorne](/wiki/Skyrim:Minorne_(book) "Skyrim:Minorne (book)")*. The book is written by Moric and extols the virtues of Minorne, who has obviously charmed everyone within the excavation except [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius"), who has been locked up for still praying to [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay").

On the left in front of a second carved head are three burial urns. The passage descends a flight of stairs to the south, and enters a split-level room containing Minorne, Moric, and one other charmed Vigilant. Wooden stairs lead down into the room. There are four large urns total in the southwest and southern corners, and wide stairs leading up to the east. At the top is a locked cage on the right that requires a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruunvald_Key "Skyrim:Ruunvald Key"), which is carried by Minorne. Florentius is in the cage; speak to him to advance the quest Bolstering the Ranks. On the lower level to the south beneath the cage is an iron door, which is also locked and requires the same key as the cage. It opens into a narrow passage, and after a couple of turns leads to a large room. Around the room is an unlocked chest against the east wall, two empty sideboards, an unowned single bed, two large urns, a stone table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a lever that raises part of the floor to reveal a spiral staircase. On the table are three random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, a poison, a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*. The stairs lead down to a narrow passage and an iron door, locked with the same key again, which leads outside to the mountains via an alternative exit a short distance south of Tolvald's Cave.

## Notes

- Before the start of the quest Bolstering the Ranks, discovering the location will not add the map marker to your map. The nearest discoverable place is Tolvald's Cave.
- The entrance only appears after the quest Bolstering the Ranks has been started, so siding with the Volkihar clan makes it impossible to enter the excavation.
  - The entrance and map marker can be enabled using the console commands `prid xx00d1fe` followed by `disable`.
  - Faction side quests for the Volkihar vampires may choose this location, even though the map marker does not appear on your map when siding with the clan.[*verification needed*]
- Once Minorne is dead, the remaining charmed Vigilants will die; however, the huskies will not.

## Bugs

- One of the crossbow traps and the barrel it is placed on can be seen clipping through a support beam.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- The copy of *Discovering Ruunvald, Vol. IV* often clips through the barrel, making it almost impossible for console players to obtain.
  - The Unrelenting Force shout or a Fireball spell can be used to push the book back toward the outer, southwest edge, where it may clip back through just enough to be grabbed.
- Sometimes upon entering Ruunvald, usually after killing the two charmed Vigilants, the game may freeze. **?**
  -  Advancing the related quest with the console should work around the problem.
- Once you have fed on any of the corpses of the charmed Vigilants in the excavation as a werewolf, you may have a permanent glowing red mist around your head, just like the charmed Vigilants.
  -  To add or remove the mist effect, use the console commands `player.addspell 02018c5d` and `player.removespell 02018c5d`.
- There are two deleted navmeshes in the vanilla DLC when inspected in TES5Edit. These deleted navmeshes are associated with the DLC1RuunvaldExterior01 cell. This is a potential related cause for reported freezing or crashing in this area of the game world. These deleted navmeshes in Dawnguard.esm are in [CELL:0000BBA5] in worldspace WRLD:0000003C at <44,-15>. **?**
- Even if you kill Minorn and loot the big chest, the location will not be seen as "cleared" **?**

## Maps

- 

  Ruunvald Excavation
- 

  Ruunvald Temple

Ruin of Saarthal

**Saarthal** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). It has two interior zones: *[Saarthal Excavation](#Saarthal_Excavation)* and *[Saarthal](#Saarthal)*.

It was the first Nord settlement in Skyrim, and is therefore a site of great interest to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), who is excavating the site in search of ancient artifacts. Unbeknownst to the college, Saarthal is also the location of the sealed tomb of [Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Jyrik Gauldurson") (part of the [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") quest).

The history of Saarthal suggests that it may have some greater significance. The original settlement was attacked by elves in the [Merethic Era](/wiki/Lore:Merethic_Era "Lore:Merethic Era"), an event known as the [Night of Tears](/wiki/Lore:Night_of_Tears "Lore:Night of Tears"). A book on the subject, *[Night of Tears](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_of_Tears "Skyrim:Night of Tears")*, suggests that the attack was actually an attempt to gain control of some powerful item found under the city. The *[Imperial Report on Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Report_on_Saarthal "Skyrim:Imperial Report on Saarthal")* also concludes that the elven attack was focused on a specific objective.

The entrance to Saarthal is locked (key required) at the start of the game. It can only be entered once you have started the quest [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal"), meaning that you must first join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") and complete its first quest, [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal")**: Uncover the mysteries beneath this ancient ruin.

### Exterior

There are series of wooden platforms and bridges with ramps leading down towards the entrance. There are many [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels on the platforms, two sets of shelves holding several [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and a table with an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") on top. Beside the shelves is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and in front are two unowned bed rolls. At the top of the last ramp is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") in the southwest corner of the excavation site.

### Saarthal Excavation

:   *This article focuses on the dungeon of Saarthal, in particular detailing the locations of all items found in the dungeon. For more detailed information about the quest that takes place here, see [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal").*

To gain entry, you must talk to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"), thus unlocking the main door. This provides you access to the first half of *Saarthal Excavation*, namely the two large chambers and connected passageways that have already been explored by the College of Winterhold. Each of the large chambers is several stories high, and dominated by ancient stone pillars. The College has built various rickety wooden ramps around the pillars, allowing you to descend into the rooms and access various sections.

In addition to various minor loot (harvested ingredients, mushrooms, leather strips) scattered throughout the area, there are a few more notable items. Next to the entrance to the first room, a bucket sitting next to a cart is hiding two [orichalcum ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ingot"). At the lowest level, on the ground against the eastern wall, there is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") to the left of some wooden scaffolding located directly beneath an overhead bridge. If you need a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") one can be found on the entry level platform, just before the first wooden pathway leading down into the excavation site. Another is on the ground level at the other side of the room from where the ore vein was found. A nearly inaccessible gate high in the northeast corner of the room prevents access to the shortcut exit from the end of the dungeon; the gate can only be opened using a handle accessible on the other side. Another iron ore vein is found on the east side of the tunnel leading to the second chamber.

The second room contains a few more valuable items. At the top-most level of the room, there is an adept-locked draugr chest. It is located due north of the entrance to the room, and requires jumping across a gap left by a collapsed bridge. On the north side of the room, at a middle level reached by a straight ramp from the room floor, there are two pieces of [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") and a [refined malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Malachite "Skyrim:Refined Malachite") ingot (the latter hidden inside a bucket). Finally, the room also contains a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"), at the middle level of the south wall, next to the circular ramp leading to the room's exit. To the left, on a ledge at the same height as the gold ore vein, reached by jumping from the start of the ramp, around the corner from it is a bucket concealing another piece of quicksilver ore.

The [Saarthal Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal_Amulet "Skyrim:Saarthal Amulet")

To move beyond the first section of the excavation, you must complete some objectives in the related quest, [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal"). The quest page provides full information on all quest-related details. However, if you wish to simply progress as quickly as possible, the key required steps are:

- Find the Ancient Amulet, on a wall at the northernmost end of the accessible area, and take it (this can be done without going through any of the quest dialogue).
- Equip the amulet, now identified in your inventory as the [Saarthal Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal_Amulet "Skyrim:Saarthal Amulet"), and cast any targeted spell at the wall where you found the amulet. The wall will crumble.
- Go through the passage leading north behind the crumbled wall to the next room. Once both you and Tolfdir are in the next room, a ghostly figure identified as [Nerien](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerien "Skyrim:Nerien") will appear with various dire warnings about the consequences of your actions.
- Talk to Tolfdir, going through his dialogue until he suggests searching the coffins.

Tolfdir's dialogue prompts the coffins in the room to burst open, releasing two leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), but also opening the passage forward. One of the two draugr is always a high-level magic-casting draugr, while the other is a standard leveled draugr specializing in one-handed melee combat. Before leaving this room, check the table in the middle of the room for a rare-type [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel").

The passage north immediately leads to a closed gate, opened by a lever on the floor to the right. The circular room on the other side of the gate has ten vertical draugr coffins along the wall at your level, and many more coffins can be seen above and below, filling a vast cylindrical chamber. Luckily, only four of the coffins contain active draugr. Once you enter the room, the four leveled archer-type draugr will burst out to attack you and Tolfdir. Although there is no loot in the room, Tolfdir is fascinated by the coffins, and stays behind in this room to study them.

Saarthal Excavation

The door out of this room leads to the next zone, *Saarthal* proper. At first, some raised spears and a lowered gate prevent you from opening the door. However, the two pull chains (one on either side of the door) make these retract. The right-hand chain also simultaneously closes the gate behind you, so you will need to activate it a second time if you want to backtrack.

**Occupants:**

- 1 leveled [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") (magic-caster; best possible level)
- 1 leveled Draugr (one-handed melee)
- 4 leveled Draugr (archers)

**Treasure:**

- 1 Chest (Draugr-type; adept locked)
- 1 [Apothecary's Satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") (rare-type)
- Ingredients: 1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 2 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 1 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota")
- Ores/Ingots: 1 [Gold Ore Vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"), 2 [Iron Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), 2 [Orichalcum Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ingot"), 3 [Quicksilver Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"), 1 [Refined Malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Malachite "Skyrim:Refined Malachite")
- Plants: 1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 4 [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), 9 [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot")
- Potions: 1 [Lingering Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Lingering_Poison "Skyrim:Lingering Poison"), 1 [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength")
- Weapons: 4 [Pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe")
- Other: 5 [Leather Strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), 1 [Lesser Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem")

### Saarthal

You start in an antechamber (with two large urns and one burial urn) that opens into the first large room of this zone. Three leveled melee draugr are waiting in their coffins, while a fourth leveled archer-type draugr is patrolling at the far end of the room and will come to help out when he hears combat. You also need to watch out for a [fire rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Elemental Rune") trap (the first of several elemental rune traps in this zone), located at the first turn in the room. Once you clear the lower level of the room, you can climb the stairs to collect the room's loot. One chest (adept-difficulty lock) is located back near the entrance to the room, on the west side of the upper level. There is also a single burial urn located next to a bookshelf on the other side of the room, which can be seen from the locked chest. The urn can be accessed by either jumping across the gap in the wood floor directly to the south of the chest, or by walking along the perimeter of the room. The other loot is all near the exit at the southeast end of the room. A small shelving unit holds a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), one [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), one leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a burial urn, and assorted clutter; another burial urn is found near the wall opposite the unit. A random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") is lying inside the broken sarcophagus in front of the door. Finally, there is one unlocked chest by the door.

Opening the iron door leads to a corridor lined with burial niches. Three burial urns are immediately across from the door. Around the corner you will see a chest at the bottom of the next section of the passage, but before rushing to the chest, note the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") on the floor, which triggers a volley of [darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Two leveled melee draugr are also waiting to ambush you from the wall niches after the chest. Two leveled restore ([health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Magicka "Skyrim:Restore Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Stamina "Skyrim:Restore Stamina")) [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") are at the end of the next section before a turn to the east; one is in the large bowl in the nook with three candle holders, and the other is in the broken urn directly opposite. The potion in the urn may be difficult to access.

The hall then leads into the first of Saarthal's two puzzles. It is a typical [pillar puzzle](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Symbol "Skyrim:Spinning Symbol"), where each pillar needs to be rotated until the symbol matches the symbol displayed on the wall behind the pillar. Once the pillars are set correctly, activating the lever opens the gate at the end of the room; if the pillars are not correct, the lever will instead trigger a dart trap. Along the north wall, the correct pillar images are (from west to east): **Eagle—Snake—Whale**. Along the south wall they are (again, from west to east): **Whale—Eagle—Eagle**. While setting the pillars, check the draugr corpses in the adjacent niches: four of the corpses can be looted for minor treasure.

Past the puzzle gate and down a set of stairs, an iron door opens into the next large room. Only one leveled draugr is on patrol at the upper level of this room: a rare female draugr, who is a two-handed melee fighter. Most of the loot (with the exception of one burial urn in the lower level) is also found in the upper level. The obvious containers in the upper level are two large urns and a burial urn. Less obvious are the two potions (one best-quality [restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") and one best-quality [restore magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Magicka "Skyrim:Restore Magicka")), both hidden in the broken urn at the northwest corner of the sarcophagus. Multiple other platforms in the room can be accessed using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"), but none of them contain anything.

The small chamber on the other side of the door contains several valuable items: an unlocked chest is flanked by a large urn on the left, and a broken urn holding a leveled sword on the right. As you push through the cobweb-filled doorway, watch out for the burial urn, lootable draugr corpse, and shock rune trap in the alcove, then a second shock rune trap as you enter the second puzzle room.

The second puzzle room contains four rotating pillars with symbols above them. The correct symbol for each pillar is shown on the wall behind the pillar (the middle section of the room also displays the correct set of symbols). The twist this time around is that activating one pillar may cause multiple pillars to rotate simultaneously. However, by observing which pillars control which other pillars, you can identify the correct order in which to set the pillars, such that once you have set a pillar, it is not altered by the subsequent pillars. The solution is:

1. Southeast pillar (Whale)
2. Northeast pillar (Snake)
3. Southwest pillar (Eagle)
4. Northwest pillar (Whale)

After confirming all four pillars are in the above positions, pull the lever to open the gate. If the pillars are not correct, you will trigger a dart trap.

Multiple rotating pillar puzzle in Saarthal

Tolfdir will catch up with you as you explore the subsequent corridor, providing a clue that you are approaching the end of the dungeon. However, you are not yet in any danger: there is one more iron door between you and the boss enemy. So first make sure to collect the loot in the corridor, while avoiding the pressure plate trap (and the darts that fly down the corridor when Tolfdir inevitably stumbles over the trap). The alcove at the north end contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), on top of which you can find a random [book](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_3 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 3") and a random restoration potion. One more random restoration potion is on the west side of the hallway, along with a leveled heavy [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a burial urn, and two lootable draugr corpses. An open sarcophagus at the south end contains a random soul gem, and another burial urn and a lootable draugr corpse are nearby.

When you are ready, open the door to reveal a large room bathed in the blue-green light of a massive orb that floats, spinning, at the far end of the room. You won't have much time to admire the sight, however, because the dungeon's boss, [Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Jyrik Gauldurson"), is also located in this room. This is where the two quests taking place in Saarthal come together: the orb is part of the Under Saarthal quest, and Jyrik is part of the [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") quest. In addition, you will need Tolfdir's help to fight Jyrik, since only Tolfdir can disable the connection between Jyrik and the orb that initially makes Jyrik invulnerable. For more details on how to defeat Jyrik, see [his page](/wiki/Skyrim:Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Jyrik Gauldurson"). Once he is killed, Saarthal is marked as [cleared](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons").

Jyrik sitting in front of the mysterious orb

Once you have dealt with Jyrik, make sure to loot his corpse to obtain a [Gauldur Amulet Fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur_Amulet_Fragment "Skyrim:Gauldur Amulet Fragment") with a +30 [Fortify Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka") enchantment and a *[Writ of Sealing](/wiki/Skyrim:Writ_of_Sealing_(Jyrik) "Skyrim:Writ of Sealing (Jyrik)")*. Reading the writ triggers the start of the [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") quest (if you had not previously started the quest). You will also want to talk to Tolfdir to receive your final objective for the Under Saarthal quest. You are then free to explore the room to find the rest of the available loot. The altar in the center of the room contains the most important items: the [Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson"), one leveled filled soul gem, and two leveled poisons, as well as a lootable draugr corpse and a burial urn. Elsewhere in the room you can find three large urns.

A door behind the orb leads to the final room of the dungeon: a fern-filled grotto that is a distinct change from the rest of the coffin-filled Nordic ruin. This room contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") (with a word of the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") shout), and the dungeon's boss chest. The exit from this room is the shortcut back to the first room of *Saarthal Excavation*. To open the final gate, you will need to activate a handle found on the east (left-hand) wall of the passage.

Saarthal

**Occupants:**

- 4 leveled [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") (one-handed melee)
- 1 leveled Draugr (archer; patrolling)
- 2 leveled Draugr (two-handed melee)
- [Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Jyrik Gauldurson") (magic-casting [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"); best possible level), carrying 1 [Gauldur Amulet Fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur_Amulet_Fragment "Skyrim:Gauldur Amulet Fragment") and 1 *[Writ of Sealing](/wiki/Skyrim:Writ_of_Sealing_(Jyrik) "Skyrim:Writ of Sealing (Jyrik)")*

**Treasure:**

- 1 Boss Chest (Draugr-type)
- 4 Chests (all Draugr-type; one locked with adept-difficulty lock)
- 8 large Urns
- 13 Burial Urns
- Armor: 1 random Heavy Armor [Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"); 1 [Steel Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield")
- Books: 1 random [Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") (from [List 3](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Books-List_3 "Category:Skyrim-Books-List 3"))
- Ingredients: 1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 1 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing")
- Plants: 5 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 14 [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss")
- Potions: 4 leveled restoration potions (equal chance of being [Restore Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health"), [Restore Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Magicka "Skyrim:Restore Magicka"), or [Restore Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Stamina "Skyrim:Restore Stamina") potions; always best possible quality), 1 best-quality [Restore Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") potion, 1 best-quality [Restore Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Magicka "Skyrim:Restore Magicka") potion, 2 random poisons (one of which is always best possible quality)
- Soul Gems: 3 random soul gems (2 are always filled; 1 has a 25% chance of being filled)
- Weapons: 1 random [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), 1 random [Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), 1 random [Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), 1 [Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson")
- Other: 1 [Coin Purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") (medium size), 1 Gold, 1 [Ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby")

**Other:**

- 1 [Alchemy Lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab")
- 1 [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") ([Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"))

## Bugs

- The pillars in the six-pillar puzzle may not move when activated.
  - This can sometimes be fixed by exiting the area and then reentering, or by reloading a save from before entering the area.
  -  On PC, you may also open the console and enter `disable 72434` to disable the gate blocking your way, or simply use `tcl` to walk directly through the gate.
  - In the final boss fight, [conjuring a flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach") may incinerate the [Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson"). To obtain the staff, re-load from an earlier save and re-run the boss fight with less fire damage.
- The containers outside of the dungeon may respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

Sacellum of Boethiah

The **Sacellum of Boethiah** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").

## Related Quests

- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.
- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").

## Walkthrough

The shrine is in the mountains east-southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It is composed of three levels, with blood stains on the ground and bloody bones and burned corpses around the shrine. If you are level 30 or higher, a number of [Boethiah Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah_Cultist "Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist") and a Priestess of Boethiah will be present; speaking to the priestess will start the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") if it has not already begun. If you approach the shrine at level 29 or below, the quest won't start, and no one will be there.

On the lowest level is a makeshift camp with a tent and three bedrolls, as well as a small arena. There are also several crates near the tent, with three bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") and a lit lantern on one of them and a small sack leaning against it. A [shovel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel") leans against another crate. Two weapon racks are in the arena, with bloody bones scattered throughout. Two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes are on this level, with one at the camp and the other in the arena. On the middle level is a tent surrounded by cages. On the left side of the tent is a burned corpse with all four [embalming tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Embalming_Tool "Skyrim:Embalming Tool") next to it. Inside the tent, there is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") to your left and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") to your right, with two [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") in between. On the highest level is the shrine, with a mysterious pillar in front of it. If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") with you inside the circle, you can activate the pillar. Tell your follower to use the pillar, and they will be drawn toward it, causing them to be trapped. This allows you to kill your follower and loot their corpse without consequence (see [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling#The_Sacrifice "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") for a workaround). A nearby unlit brazier holds two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). On the other side is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), with a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") and a [weak stamina poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison") nearby.

Two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") are 300 feet south-southwest of the Sacellum, next to a small animal den. You can also find sixteen snowberry bushes, eight [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), three [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), and a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") on your way up the hill.

The Daedric carvings

The magic pillar is surrounded by spiral [Daedric carvings](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Alphabet "Lore:Daedric Alphabet") on the ground, with a magical channel that lights up when you enter its zone. The Daedric carvings are mirrored, and must be read from the outside to the center. Translated into the Latin alphabet, the text reads as follows:

:   I am alive because that one is dead
    I e[x]ist because I have the will to do so

This is a direct quote from the book *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")*.

## Notes

- As you climb the mountain path to the shrine, no matter what time of day it is, the sky will darken rapidly as if it were night. Nevertheless, music that plays during the day will still play here during daytime hours.

## Bugs

- The sky may not darken as you make your way to the shrine. Also, if you go back down the hill during the day to revert the sky to its normal state, then immediately turn around and go back up the hill, the sky may remain bright and not darken again. **?**
- The weapons in the arena may be hovering in the air in front of their respective weapon racks. **?**

Sadri's Used Wares

**Sadri's Used Wares** is a general shop in the Gray Quarter of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

It is owned by [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri"), a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") trader and common level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") for [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech"). It consists of one area only, *[Sadri's Used Wares](#Sadri.27s_Used_Wares)*.

**NOTE**: Like all other stores, Sadri's Used Wares has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main trading room. These can be bought from the proprietor and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Speech (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Speech (Common)") |

## Related Quests

- **[That Was Always There](/wiki/Skyrim:That_Was_Always_There "Skyrim:That Was Always There")**: Return a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola%27s_Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Viola's Gold Ring") to its rightful [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano").

## Sadri's Used Wares

Inside Sadri's Used Wares

Without the displayed merchandise the main trading room becomes quite empty and consists mostly of valuable kitchen utensils. The huge counter has a copy of *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")* on top and, hidden behind the counter, a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*. A few weapons are hung on the southeastern wall, including an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), along with three shields, an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"). Through the doorway to the south is a storage room with a wardrobe with random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"), an end table with clutter, and the store's [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on a set of shelves.

The doorway to the north leads to Sadri's private quarters where he sleeps every night between midnight and 8am. The southwestern corner contains a small table with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and some [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"). Along the western wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). The adjacent corner has two food sacks and some shelves with several items, including an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a sample of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and the [Business Ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"). The owned bed stands along the northern wall, with a handy bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") next to the pillow. The northeastern corner has a wardrobe with some assorted clothes. A dresser along the eastern wall contains clothes and has another bottle of wine and a bottle of Nord mead on top.

## Displayed Merchandise

- The following items are sitting out in the store on counters, shelves, or tables. They can be purchased or taken for free if your [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with Sadri is high enough. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Weapons**: 1 [Iron Mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") - **Apparel**: 1 [Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), 1 [Fine Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), 1 [Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), 1 [Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") - **Potions**: 1 [Draught of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), 1 [Draught of Vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Draught of Vigor"), 2 [Frostbite Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), 1 [Philter of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Philter of Resist Fire"), 1 [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"), 1 [Solution of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Solution of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Solution of Lasting Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Solution of Lasting Potency"), 1 [Solution of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Solution of Regeneration"), 1 [Solution of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength") - **Ingredients**: 4 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 1 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), 1 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") - **Books**: 1 *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Lore:Beggar_Prince "Lore:Beggar Prince")*, 1 *[Chance's Folly](/wiki/Lore:Chance%27s_Folly "Lore:Chance's Folly")*, 1 *[The Monomyth](/wiki/Lore:The_Monomyth "Lore:The Monomyth")*, 1 *[The Wolf Queen, v2](/wiki/Lore:The_Wolf_Queen "Lore:The Wolf Queen")*, 1 *[Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Yngol_and_the_Sea-Ghosts "Lore:Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts")* - **Misc**: 1 [Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") |

## Bugs

- If [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri") dies, [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") technically becomes owner of Sadri's Used Wares. However, he never takes over running the store: he never enters the store, and even if he were to enter the store, he does not own the store's merchant chest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") has been selected to fill the backup alias and will take over when Revyn dies.

# Skyrim:Saering's Watch

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") |

Saering's Watch

**Saering's Watch** is a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") in the shadow of [Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches the first word of the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal")**: Find a way to free the citizens of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

## Walkthrough

Word wall

Should you come here from [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") up the hill southeast of Saering's Watch, you'll pass under two arches before coming upon the lair, where the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") (appearing after [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")) and [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will almost always be locked in battle. Unless you're up for some jumping, you'll have to enter from the northwest, navigating around some rubble. On the east-northeast and southeast sides of this small courtyard are hut-like structures, the former of which contains an unlocked chest.

Stairs are to the southwest, with a broken shelving unit at the base of the stairs holding a potion. The right-hand stairs lead up to a hut-like structure containing three random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), two random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (one filled and one empty), and an overlook from which a draugr may snipe at the dragon and/or you. The left-hand stairs lead up to the second level, which contains two upright sarcophagi, one of which is around the corner to the right. If the dragon is here, these will be open already; if not, they will burst open as you arrive on this level. The third level has the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), which teaches the first word for the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), and a boss chest. Across from the stairs is another upright draugr sarcophagus. In front of the word wall, a dead skeleton surrounded by candles lies on a table, with two [fire enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") swords laid across it in a cross shape. A random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") and a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") are on the ground beside the table.

## Notes

- The dragon shout word can be learned without the quest active or the [Dragonborn questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Quests#Main_Quest "Skyrim:Dragonborn Quests") even started.
- This is the only dragon lair that [bounty quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon") and [dragon hunts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting") won't assign you to.
- At high levels, past 30 or so, the dragon/draugr battle can result in a stalemate, as any Draugr Deathlords will frequently bombard the dragon with Unrelenting Force. This can work to your advantage.
- You can use the structures of Searing's Watch itself to help defeat the dragon. If you use archery or ranged spells, there is a lot of cover, and not enough space for the dragon to land, so you can easily snipe it.
- If you drop in from the mountains to the south, you can get the shout and leave again without ever triggering the dragon.
- If the Dragonborn questline is started but not completed, [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") may steal the dragon's soul here each time the location respawns.

# Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **[Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") asks you to deliver some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron") |
| Reward: | [Potion of Brief Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), [Potion of Enhanced Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), [Potion of Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Potion of Illusion") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Farengar, Arcadia) |
| ID: | FreeformWhiterunQuest05 |

Does he need a love elixir?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire").
2. Talk to [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia").

### The Only Show In Town

[Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") is a dedicated [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard") serving [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") at [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Most of his time is spent studying and advising the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") on the current [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") threat.
However, he does have time to assist the locals in town. If you ask him if he is the only wizard in town, he will acknowledge that while, technically, he is alone in his craft, the town also holds other practitioners. And, since he's on the subject, he remembers he has some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar%27s_Frost_Salt "Skyrim:Farengar's Frost Salt") he'd promised to pick up for local alchemist [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia"), the proprietor of [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"). He asks if you wouldn't mind delivering the frost salts; Arcadia will surely compensate you for them. When you tell him you will help him out, he will respond with a disparaging remark, but will hand you the frost salts, a quest item not to be dropped.

### He'll Never Know What Hit Him

Head to Arcadia's Cauldron and enter during regular business hours, specifically between 8am and 8pm, or even when she strolls around the main trading room in the evening; as always, she will claim you have a fatal [disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Disease "Skyrim:Disease") in hopes you will buy one of her potions, but will be grateful for the salts. She then reveals she needs the salts for a love elixir meant for the unsuspecting Farengar, and will then hand you three [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") as compensation. Additionally, as you have now earned her [friendship](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"), almost all the various [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and potions in her shop are free to take.

## Quest Stages

| Salt for Arcadia (FreeformWhiterunQuest05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Give the Frost Salts to Arcadia |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformWhiterunQuest05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformWhiterunQuest05`.

# Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder") |
| Location(s): | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder")) |
| ID: | FreeformShipsDawnstar |

Captain Wayfinder and his crew

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder") on his ship at the dock in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
2. Retrieve the [salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") from the given location.
3. Return to Captain Wayfinder and receive your reward.

### Captain Wayfinder

In central Dawnstar, you will find the ship [The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall") permanently docked, with inexperienced sailor [Captain Wayfinder](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder") and his team of disrespectful crewmembers wandering around on deck. Talk to Wayfinder and ask him about the ship and he will provide a bit of background information on his questionable status as captain. He will also hint at problems with his latest shipment, some [fine-cut void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") that have gone missing. When asked what happened to the salts he will reveal: *"Sailors are what happened to them. They got drunk and ended up losing the merchandise in some cave. If you're not afraid of little exploring, I'll pay good gold to get those salts."*

### Find the Salts

At this point, it is no longer possible to reject the favor and a map marker will point towards one of eight radiant locations.

**Possible locations**: [Brood Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Brood_Cavern "Skyrim:Brood Cavern") • [Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn") • [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave") • [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl") • [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb") • [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn") • [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") • [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")

Travel to the selected location and locate the fine-cut void salts in the boss-leveled chest, then head back to Dawnstar and the Sea Squall.

When you hand him the salts, a grateful Captain Wayfinder will hand you a leveled amount of gold, with his thanks: *"That's the first bit of good news I've had since I set sail a year ago. Here's your cut."*

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, this quest is referred to as **Salt of the Seas**.
- The fine-cut void salts that you are asked to find are actually just regular [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), except it is a unique sample of the salts that have been given a different name.
- All eight samples of fine-cut void salts spawn in the possible locations when you first visit Dawnstar. Finding them will not start the quest and only the sample indicated after speaking to Wayfinder will function as a quest item and net you the reward.
- If the game decides to send you to a location where you already found the salts, and you still have the original sample in your inventory, a new sample will spawn at the location, but you will miss out on the map marker.
- If you find any of the samples before starting the quest, the fine-cut version can be consumed like normal void salts.
  - Trying to consume the salts selected for the quest results in the rather rare error message "You cannot eat quest items."

## Bugs

- The fine-cut void salts may stay in your inventory after receiving the payment and finishing the quest. This often happens if you have regular [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") in your inventory (or if you carry another sample of the fine-cut version) when you return to Captain Wayfinder. They are no longer a quest item.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- It's possible to run across a second batch of fine-cut void salts in another location. If you've already completed the quest, you can turn them in again for another reward.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- If you find a sample of Fine-Cut Void Salts prior to obtaining the quest, it will automatically put the quest in your Miscellaneous log. If you then speak to Captain Wayfinder and pick any topic other than, "I have the Fine-Cut Void Salts", he will finish his dialogue and then never speak to you again, making it impossible to finish the quest. This can sometimes be fixed by using the console command `setstage freeformshipsDawnstar 20`. When it works, this ends the quest and removes the fine-cut void salts from your inventory.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformShipsDawnstar stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformShipsDawnstar`.

# Skyrim:Salvius Farm

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Wheat Mill.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Wheat_Mill.png) | Wheat Mill: Salvius Farm ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Salvius+Farm)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SalviusFarmhouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") North of [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") | |

Salvius Farm

**Salvius Farm** is a small farm east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [Vigdis Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigdis_Salvius "Skyrim:Vigdis Salvius") and [Rogatus Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") tend the farm and live in the Farmhouse.

The farm itself contains 17 [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants and three [chicken nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). Three [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") can be found around the walls of the farm and many [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") can be harvested nearby.

Rogatus will ask you to deliver a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter") for him, while [Vigdis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigdis_Salvius "Skyrim:Vigdis Salvius") runs the farm and will pay for any harvested potatoes.

## Residents

Salvius Farmhouse

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Rogatus Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius")  [Vigdis Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigdis_Salvius "Skyrim:Vigdis Salvius") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rogatus's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter")**: Deliver a letter to a [farmer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius").

## Notes

- Just to the east of the farm by the signpost adjacent to the bridge is the camping site for [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad")'s [caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders").

## Bugs

- The chicken may not be marked as owned by the farm.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- The Imperial guard who patrols near the farm is called "Markarth City Guard", even though he isn't in the city.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The guard is now called "Reach Hold Guard".
