# Skyrim:Sanctuary

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Pick up your first contracts as a [Brotherhood member](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Members "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") |
| Reward: | The [Shrouded Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"), [Shrouded Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hood "Skyrim:Shrouded Hood"), [Shrouded Hand Wraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hand_Wraps "Skyrim:Shrouded Hand Wraps"), and [Shrouded Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Shoes "Skyrim:Shrouded Shoes") |
| ID: | DB02a |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") | **Next →** [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") | | → Next | [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | | |

Nazir has some contracts for you

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Finish talking to [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid").
2. Meet your new family members.
3. Speak to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") and pick up your contracts.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After speaking to [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid"), turn back and search the shelves for a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Sithis](/wiki/Skyrim:Sithis "Skyrim:Sithis")*, and a set of [shrouded robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"). Enter the room behind the map table and pick up the [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), sitting on the dresser to the left, for the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned").

### A Happy Little Family

*"Would the sweetie like a sweetie?"*

Descend the steps by Astrid and join the other members in listening to [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") recounting her last contract. After she tells her tale the others will have a light-hearted banter about how difficult each others contracts were, highlighting how dysfunctional the little "family" really is:

**[Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn")**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**[Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara")**: *"Ha ha ha ha! Again! Again! Do the part where he tries to buy you some candy."*
**[Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette")**: *"Okay, okay. Wait. Here we go. "Ooh, you are such a pretty little girl. Would the sweetie like a sweetie? Oh yes, how about some chocolate?" Oh yes, please, kind sir. My mama and papa left me all alone, and I'm so very hungry. I know a shortcut to the candy shop. Through this alley. Oh ya, very good. Very good. My it is dark down here. Oh, but you are so beautiful. Such a lovely smile. Your teeth... your teeth! No! Aggghh!!"*
**[Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella")**: *"Oh Babette, but you are so wicked."*
**[Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir")**: *"What about you, Festus? How did that last contract turn out?"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"Oh, yes, please, old man. Regale us with your tales of wizardry..."*
**[Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex")**: *"Ah, the young and stupid. Always mocking the experienced and brilliant. My contract went very well, I'll have you know. Tried a new spell. Little something I've been working on in my spare time. Came "this" close to turning that priest inside out. Damned messy."*
**Gabriella**: *"And what of your latest, Arnbjorn. Something about a Khajiit? Merchant was it?"*
**Babette**: *"Oh, a big doggy chasing a little kitty! How adorable!"*
**Nazir**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Festus**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Veezara**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"I am not adorable, it was not funny, and he wasn't a merchant. He was a Khajiit monk, a master of the Whispering Fang style. But now he's dead... and I have a new loincloth."*

### Accepting the Contract

When the gathering breaks up, move to the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") to the north of the room and absorb the word for the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout. If you pass near Babette she will remark *"Heard she pulled the ole' "Choose your victim" gag with you. Ah, I love that one..."*, shedding some light as to the real victim of the previous quest.

:   *When you accept a contract you will be unable to interact normally with your target, preventing you from completing any quests involving them. Check the notes section before taking any contracts.*

Nazir moves to the brazier near the pool and awaits your "valued" input. No matter what way the discussion proceeds, he will mock your talents, going as far as saying *"I have no intention of getting invested in someone who may be dead tomorrow."* Finish speaking to Nazir to pick up your first contracts. There are three assassination jobs. You can do each one at a time and return for payment, or you can do all three and return to Nazir once completed. The three contracts are for [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") and [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild").

## Notes

- Narfi is involved in the quest [The Straw that Broke](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Straw_that_Broke "Skyrim:The Straw that Broke"). Therefore, once the contract is accepted, it will not be possible to complete this quest.
- You do not have to listen to the gathering. If you talk to Nazir straight away, the group breaks up, however this is the only time this conversation is heard.
- The non-armor version of the Shrouded Armor consists of [Hand Wraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hand_Wraps "Skyrim:Shrouded Hand Wraps"), a [Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hood "Skyrim:Shrouded Hood"), [Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"), and [Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Shoes "Skyrim:Shrouded Shoes"). These are the clothing version of the armor, which is designed for mages. The [Maskless Cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Cowl_Maskless "Skyrim:Shrouded Cowl Maskless") sitting with them is considered to be [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor").

It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB02a`.

# Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **End the dispute over [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") or [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar") |
| Location(s): | [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold (medium), [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") if side with [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"))  =1 ([Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"))  =1 ([Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar"))  or  =-1 ([Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"))  =-1 ([Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"))  =-1 ([Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar")) |
| ID: | FreeformKarthwastenA |

.jpg)

Help resolve a local dispute

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") about the troubles with [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine").
2. Talk to [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar") about why he shut the mine down.
3. Convince Ainethach to sell the mine, or convince Atar to leave.

### Miner Extortion

When you first enter [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), you will see the townsfolk squaring off against a group of [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary") sent by the [Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood") family in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to secure the mine after a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") incident. [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"), the owner of the mine, is arguing with [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar"), the leader of the mercenary band:

**Ainethach**: *"I want you sellswords out of my mine."*
**Atar**: *"Watch your tongue, native. We'll leave when we're sure there's no Forsworn here."*
**Ainethach**: *"Oh, and when would that be, I wonder? When I sell my land to the Silver-Bloods?"*
**Atar**: *"The Silver-Bloods have made you a very generous offer for this pile of dirt. I suggest you take it."*

The Silver-Bloods are demanding that the mine be signed over to them in return for the protection they provided in the last attack. The mercenaries have been instructed to prevent anyone from returning to work in the Sauranach Mine until the rights to it are signed over to the Silver-Blood family.

### Deciding to Help Ainethach

Ainethach should be standing on the porch of his house during the day, and once approached he will agree to let you help him, and will ask you to convince Atar to leave. Unless you catch up to the band before they go into the mine, you will need to enter the mine to find Atar in the far end, standing on a raised platform.

#### Talking to Atar

After agreeing to help Ainethach enter the mine and speak with Atar. When you ask him to leave you will be given three options.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| This whole town wants you out. Leave. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Dealing with a mob wouldn't be good for my coin purse. Fine. We're leaving. **Failed**: Let's see them make us. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Ainethach **Failed**: Nothing |
| You'll listen to gold, I take it? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: That I will, stranger. This is more than the Silver-Bloods are paying us. We'll clear out. **Failed**: Don't think I'm being paid already? Get lost. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Ainethach **Failed**: Nothing |
| I think I'll just kill you. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Whoa. Wait a second. I was just kidding. We'll leave. We'll leave! **Failed**: I thought today was going to be boring. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Ainethach **Failed**: Attack |
| On second thought, I'll be leaving. | Milk drinker. | | | | Nothing |

After successfully convincing him, you will have to run back to Ainethach to tell him the good news, whereupon he will give you your cut.

Note that even after successfully persuading, bribing, or intimidating, the mercenaries will claim that the mine is theirs, and will warn against sudden movements. There is no bounty for killing the mercenaries even after they agree to leave.

#### Strong Arm Tactics

An alternative option is to not talk to Atar at all, but to simply kill all the mercenaries. There are no mages or archers in the group, just weak melee fighters and the somewhat more formidable Atar, who is equipped as a bandit chief with leveled heavy armor, heavy shield, and one-handed weapon. The mercenary outside the mine will still greet you with pleasantries even after taking this option. There is no bounty for killing the mercenaries inside the mine, even if you attack first.

### Selling Out

You can also remedy the situation by speaking to Atar who will offer you a cut of the purchase price if you can convince Ainethach to sell. You have to talk to Ainethach, and will be given the usual persuade, bribe, intimidate options if you tell him "I think you should sell the mine".

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| They won't stop until you do. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: You're right. They always get what they want, somehow. Fine. Tell Atar I'll sell. **Failed**: Someone has to stand up to them. I won't sell. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Atar **Failed**: Nothing |
| Look. I'll give you a fair price. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: That's more gold than they're offering. Fine. I'll sell. **Failed**: This isn't about the money. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Atar **Failed**: Nothing |
| You do or you get hurt. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Easy. I'll sell. Just don't hurt anyone. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Atar |
| Forget it, then. | Let's do that. | | | | Nothing |

After successfully convincing him, you will have to run back to Atar to tell him the good news, whereupon he will give you your cut.

### Reward

The reward is the same regardless of which path you choose to take, a medium amount of leveled gold. Don't miss the seven [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") in the mine and the leveled shield that Atar carries (if you decide to kill the mercenaries).

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- Siding with Ainethach will cause Ainethach's, [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh")'s and [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar")'s dispositions towards you to rise to 1.
  - Siding with Atar will cause Ainethach's, Lash gra-Dushnikh's, and Ragnar's dispositions towards you to fall to -1.

## Bugs

- When leaving Sanuarach Mine, a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") corpse may randomly appear in front of the mine left of the smelter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. The corpse will no longer appear in front of the mine.
- Ainethach's dialogue at the end of the quest does not exit with a goodbye flag.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.
- If you make Ainethach sell the mine by brawl, there's no further dialogue with him and you have no other choice but to help Ainethach.

## Quest Stages

| Sanuarach Mine (FreeformKarthwastenA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Convince Atar to leave Sauranach Mine |
| 25 |  | *Objective 30:* Tell Ainethach that Atar has been dealt with |
| 30 |  | *Objective 10 or 20:* Convince Atar to leave Sauranach *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Mine *or* Convince Ainethach to sell Saunaruch *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Mine |
| 35 |  | *Objective 40:* Tell Atar that Ainethach has been dealt with |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 7, 8, 10, 100, 200, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformKarthwastenA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformKarthwastenA`.

# Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Mine: Sanuarach Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sanuarach+Mine)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Silver-Blood Mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KarthwastenSanuarachMine | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 7 |

Sanuarach Mine

**Sanuarach Mine** is a small [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northern [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") initially containing [Silver-Blood mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary"). It contains only one zone, *[Sanuarach Mine](#Sanuarach_Mine)*.

The settlement and its two mines are owned by [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"), but the brutish mercenary [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar") is attempting to force Ainethech to sell the properties to the [Silver-Blood family](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood#Silver-Blood_Family "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The situation may be resolved in the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)").

## Related Quests

- **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)")**: End the dispute over Sanuarach Mine.

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), a cart with three pieces of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), and a [Juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") tree on a rock are outside the mine entrance. When you first visit the settlement, you will find the residents squaring off against Atar and the Silver-Blood mercenaries in front of the mine. On subsequent visits, a [Markarth guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth Guard") will be in front of the mine entrance.

### Sanuarach Mine

Upon entering, a ramp leads down to a junction. On your left are two small shelving units holding three [iron helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), two [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), two [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), and a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"). Taking the eastern path to the right and following the path on the bottom level, you will find a silver ore vein on the ground. Still along the eastern path, at the top of a wooden ramp are two silver ore veins on the left wall. Another wooden ramp ascends to three more silver ore veins, again on the left wall.

The western path opens into a cavern with a large wooden structure, in front of which are two archery targets and a low table holding two [long bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). On the left is a wooden ramp leading up to a dining area with two tables holding [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). The table on the left holds a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), with two garlic braids, two [dried elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and a sample of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging above. The other table holds four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"). Another double wooden ramp leads up to the final silver ore vein on the right wall.

## Notes

- If you haven't completed the quest Sanuarach Mine, one Silver-Blood mercenary will patrol the eastern path, a second mercenary will patrol from the junction to the cavern along the western path, and a third mercenary and Atar will be in the cavern.
- The silver ore veins can be mined regardless of whether you complete the quest Sanuarach Mine.
- Sanuarach Mine also [appears](/wiki/Online:Sanuarach_Mine "Online:Sanuarach Mine") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- When leaving Sanuarach Mine, a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") corpse may randomly appear in front of the mine left of the smelter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. The corpse will no longer appear in front of the mine.

Sarethi Farm

**Sarethi Farm** is a farm east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") that cultivates [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). It contains only one zone, *[Sarethi Farm](#Sarethi_Farm)*.

After the eruption of the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"), the Sarethis moved to [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") and founded this farm. Their daughter [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") once studied as an apprentice in [Skingrad](/wiki/Lore:Skingrad "Lore:Skingrad") under [Sinderion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion"). He randomly showed up on the farm and set up a field research lab there for several decades. In exchange, he taught Avrusa everything he knew about Nirnroot, leading to her unique ability to cultivate the elusive plant.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | [Aduri Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aduri_Sarethi "Skyrim:Aduri Sarethi")  [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") | | | [Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") | | --- | | [Imperial Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") \*  [Rift Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Guard "Skyrim:Rift Guard") | |

\* Only appears if the Rift is taken by the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)") or [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.
- **[Smooth Jazbay](/wiki/Skyrim:Smooth_Jazbay "Skyrim:Smooth Jazbay")**: Collect 20 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") for [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi").

### Exterior

| Crops | Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 7 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  12 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 8 [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 1 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

There are a further three gourds in a cart by the crops.

### Sarethi Farm

Farmhouse interior

You enter into a room with a cooking pot and a small table with two chairs opposite you, and a set of double doors on your left. On the table are a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). There is a dresser with two samples of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top, to the right of the exit with a barrel next to it. There is a large set of shelves on the west wall, with an open crate on the floor between the shelves and the barrel. There is also a staircase down to the basement with a barrel in the corner above them. In the open crate are two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), jazbay grapes, two [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), two more lavender, a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"). On the shelves are three gourds, three loaves of bread, two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an eidar cheese wedge, two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), eight potatoes, a [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Hanging above the dresser are two of each [dried elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

Bedroom

Through the double doors is a double bedroom containing two single beds against the north wall, a chest in front of the bed on the left, a barrel and wardrobe opposite, and a wall shelf on your right all as you enter. There is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") under the bed on the right. The wall shelf holds two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

Downstairs

Downstairs is an alchemy lab, a single bed, a small set of shelves containing a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison"), a [philter of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Philter of Extra Magicka"), a [restore health potion recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Restore Health Potion Recipe"), a [paralysis poison recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison_Recipe "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison Recipe"), and an alto wine. There is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") under the stairs. Next to the alchemy lab is an open crate containing a lavender, two [deathbells](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"). There is a dresser with a copy of *[Spirit of Nirn](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_Nirn "Skyrim:Spirit of Nirn")* on top, and finally another large set of shelves containing two Nirnroot, two [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a tundra cotton, an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), a bleeding crown, a blue mountain flower, a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), a [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a dried elves ear, two [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and deathbell. Above the lab is a wall shelf containing two Nord mead and two sacks.

## Notes

- Two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are west of the farm on the far side of a pond. A third iron ore vein is to the north-northeast.
- Eight Nirnroot plants are within the fences outside, representing the densest concentration of Nirnroot in the game.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the 3 gourds in the cart as owned by the farm.

## Bugs

- After completing [A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots"), [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") was supposed to start growing some [Crimson Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline is completed in favor of the Empire, an [Imperial soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") will appear to guard the farm, but the Stormcloak-aligned Rift guard will not be removed. This results in a fight to the death between the two.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The guards at the farm aren't linked to their XMarkers and thus would not patrol the area.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- The door is locked night and day, and no key exists. If you marry [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi"), you will need to pick the lock every time you want to go into your wife's house, and the presence of the guard means that you can be arrested for it.

# Skyrim:Saturalia Preparation

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Track down a traveling merchant to take part in end-of-year festivities.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Saturalia Holiday Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | Camp north of [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | ccVSVSSE001\_MainQuest |
| Added by: | [Saturalia Holiday Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack") |

A festival merchant has come to Skyrim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Agrane Peryval](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrane_Peryval "Skyrim:Agrane Peryval") at his camp north of [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins").

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Saturalia Holiday Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. Nevertheless, the rewards can still be bought from [Agrane Peryval](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrane_Peryval "Skyrim:Agrane Peryval").**

This short quest will be added to your journal upon installing the [Saturalia Holiday Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). You will be directed to locate a merchant who has set up shop near [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") in advance of [Saturalia](/wiki/Lore:Saturalia "Lore:Saturalia"), a festival which takes place on the 25th of [Evening Star](/wiki/Lore:Evening_Star "Lore:Evening Star"). Note that the in-game time of year is irrelevant for the purposes of this quest.

The merchant's camp can be found just outside Dawnstar, north of the [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins"). It is located close to a [World Interaction](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") spawn point which may prove problematic. The merchant is [Agrane Peryval](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrane_Peryval "Skyrim:Agrane Peryval"), who can be found at the camp along with a tame [reindeer](/wiki/Skyrim:Reindeer "Skyrim:Reindeer"). Simply speak to Agrane to finish the quest; you are under no obligation to buy anything from him.

If you do choose to make a purchase, his stock includes several unique items: three sets of festive clothing ([Saturalia Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Boots "Skyrim:Saturalia Boots"), [Saturalia Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Clothes "Skyrim:Saturalia Clothes"), [Saturalia Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Gloves "Skyrim:Saturalia Gloves")) and a [bill of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Reindeer_Bill_of_Sale "Skyrim:Reindeer Bill of Sale") for the nearby reindeer. Once purchased, the reindeer can be used as a mount, and will return to this camp if you switch to another mount.

## Quest Stages

| Saturalia Preparation (ccVSVSSE001\_MainQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Saturalia is coming soon, and there are rumors of a new merchant up near Dawnstar who sells very rare and unique wares just for the holiday. I should go look for him. *Objective 0:* Find the Saturalia merchant |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccVSVSSE001_MainQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccVSVSSE001_MainQuest`.

# Skyrim:Scare my Enemy

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Assault a target.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") |
| Location(s): | Radiant |
| Reward: | 50 gold |
| ID: | WIAssault02 |

Teach someone a lesson

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Activate the letter you received.
2. Speak with its writer.
3. Assault the target.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Every time you hit someone, or trigger an "assault", you might trigger this quest. Someone will hear about the assault and send [a letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Request_from "Skyrim:Request from") requesting that you come to see them. To start the quest you need to drop the letter and pick it up, then read it. Seek out the person requesting your presence, and they will ask you to hurt someone, maybe even kill them. They will offer to pay you, but will not help if you get caught by any guards. You can refuse the request if you wish.

As the target is usually a normal citizen, it is advisable to not use a weapon when attacking those targets you are not requested to kill, as they do not have much health or defense. Using your hands, or shield-bashing them should be sufficient to complete the task without killing them. Return to your employer and they will be thrilled that you have completed the task, sometimes wondering if there was lots of blood or screaming. Alternatively if you accidentally killed your target when not requested, they will be horrified or scared that it will be traced back to them, and refuse to pay you.

## Dialogue

When you first approach the NPC:

:   **You wanted to see me about something?**

They can say:

- *"I heard you attacked someone in town recently. Thought you might be open to doing it again... for a tidy sum."*
- *"Heard you hit somebody in town not too long ago. I'll pay to do the same, to a certain special someone."*
- *"So you like to hurt people, huh? The town is still talking about what you did. You know, I'll pay you to attack one of my enemies..."*
- *"Yeah. You beat people up. Got someone I want you to hurt. Don't worry, I can pay."*
- *"Uh... yeah. I know you don't mind hurting people. Just look what you did to... well, you know. I need someone to do that to someone. I'll even pay."*
- *"I heard you hurt someone in town not too long ago. I'll pay you to hurt someone else. Okay?"*
- *"I heard about what you did. You hurt someone. Bad. I got someone who deserves a beating, but I need someone else to do it for me. I can pay."*
- *"Yeah. Uh, I know you hurt someone in town recently. I'd like to pay you to hurt somebody else. For me."*

You can then reply with:

:   **I don't mind hurting someone for money.**

- *"No funerals, just some pain. If you get caught, it's not my problem."*
- *"No killing. I'm not hiring the Dark Brotherhood, here. If you get caught, it's not my problem."*
- *"Just cause some pain. I don't want a death on my conscience. If you get caught, it's not my problem."*
- *"Hurt him. I mean her. Whichever. No killing though. And I ain't paying your fine if you get caught."*
- *"I hope I can hear the screams. But don't let on it's from me! And I'm not paying your fine if you get caught."*
- *"Make it quick, but make it hurt. If you get caught by the guards, I don't know you."*
- *"Good. No killing, though. Don't get arrested. I won't help you."*
- *"Make it hurt. But not too much. No killing. And don't let the guards catch you."*
- *"It should hurt. A lot. But I'm not paying for murder. Oh, if you're caught, it's not my problem."*
- *"Good. Now remember - pain, and lots of it. But not to the death. If they arrest you, it's not my problem."*

If you decline:

:   **Doesn't sound like something I'm interested in.**
:   *"That's too bad."*

If you accepted and speak to them again before the assault:

:   *"You have a job to do."*
:   *"You want to get paid? Do what I hired you for."*

If you kill the person:

:   **I ended up killing your enemy.**

- *"They're dead? But now everyone will think I did it!"*
- *"What have you done? You weren't supposed to murder anyone! Gods..."*
- *"Good. Wait. Dead? That's not what I asked for. I... uh... you should leave. I need a drink..."*
- *"Dead? No, no, no, no, no! This is terrible. I don't know you. Get away from me!"*
- *"Shor's bones! What did you do that for? I would have hired the Dark Brotherhood if I'd wanted that! Get away from me."*
- *"Really? What did you go and do that for? You... you need to go away."*
- *"No! Tell me you're joking. Sweet Mara, what have I done? Go away. Just go away."*
- *"Oh gods, what did you do that for? This is horrible. I'm not paying for murder. Get away from me."*
- *"What have you done? They'll think I did it. Wait, I did do it! I'm not paying you! This is all your fault!"*

If you were successful:

:   **I did what you asked.**

- *"Ha! There's nothing like a few cuts and bruises to drive home a point, huh?"*
- *"Good. Maybe things will be different around here from now on."*
- *"Good. Let's hope it's a lesson learned."*
- *"You what? Oh. That. Good. I hope there was a lot of blood."*
- *"It can't be traced back to me, can it? Was there lot's of crying? I hope so."*
- *"Really? I hope it hurt."*
- *"Hmph. Good. That'll teach 'em."*
- *"Really? Good. Was there a lot of screaming? Never mind. I don't want to know."*
- *"Were there tears? I hope everyone can see the bruises."*
- *"Good. I hope it hurt a lot, after all the pain I've been put through."*

## Bugs

- The script on the letter you receive is incomplete. Simply reading the letter will not activate the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - To start the quest, you must drop the letter and pick it up again. The letter brings up a debug message when picked up stating that the quest start script needs to be added when books are fully implemented.
    - As part of partial mitigation, the debug message was previously removed in version 1.0 of the Unofficial Skyrim Patch. [*verification needed*]
- Some NPCs consider "friendly" spells like Heal Other to be an assault, presenting you with a safe way of completing the quest without killing the target.
- If you choose to turn down the job, the NPC may hand you 50 gold and the misc. quest objective to "Meet <radiant NPC> in <radiant location> about a job involving violence." may become stuck in your quest log. Using the setstage command may not work.
- Even if the quest requires you not to kill the target, you will still be successful if you kill the target.
- You can receive the reward even if you decline the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, addresses this issue. It also prevents receiving the reward if you kill the target.
- Sometimes, the objective "Report success to <Alias=QuestGiver>" will not disappear from quest log.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  -  To get rid of this log entry use the command `CompleteAllObjectives WIAssault02`.
- Children are not immune from being targets.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=16217))
- The Male Commoner voice and/or the Male Coward voice are incorrectly used in this quest. [*verification needed*]
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.5, fixes this bug.
- This quest can incorrectly pay out rewards even if you kill the target (usually not what the NPC asked for) or if you refuse the quest (obviously shouldn't do that).
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.

# Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [MistahFixIt](/w/index.php?title=User:MistahFixIt&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:MistahFixIt (page does not exist)"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") |
| Location(s): | [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"), [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), [Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto") |
| Reward: | Assorted [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"); Upgraded Thieves Guild Armor. |
| ID: | TG04 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits") | **Next →** [Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits") | | → Next | [Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence") | | |

The East Empire Warehouse

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey").
2. (Optional) Speak to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf").
3. Speak to [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei").
4. Retrieve a [case of Firebrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebrand_Wine_Case "Skyrim:Firebrand Wine Case") from the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").
5. Return to Gulum-Ei.
6. Follow him from a safe distance.
7. Confront *or* negotiate with Gulum-Ei.
8. Return to Mercer.

### The Plot Thickens

When you next speak to Mercer, he will remark that the symbol found on the [Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)") from [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") is the same as the one on the [Promissory Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Promissory_Note "Skyrim:Promissory Note") found at the [Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery"), leading him to the conclusion that the Thieves Guild is not, in fact, cursed (as [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") believes) but is in fact being deliberately acted against by an unknown competitor. Mercer will also reveal that a name mentioned on the Bill is the alias of a former contact of the Guild: an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") dockworker for the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") named [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei").

### Nothing Gets You Nothing

Mercer will send you to the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to shake down Gulum-Ei for information regarding the sale of Goldenglow Estate: namely, its purchaser. However, Gulum-Ei is used to dealing with Thieves Guild thugs, and will not forfeit his information easily, out of fear for his own safety. To successfully persuade him, you need a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of at least 75 (or 53 with the persuasion perk). Intimidation will always fail.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Identify the buyer and we'll forget what we know. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: All right. Had I known the deal would bring me this much trouble, I never would have accepted the gold. **Failed**: I don't care what you promise. If I tell you the buyer's name and word gets around, it could ruin me! | | | | **Passed**: Identify the buyer **Failed**: Nothing |
| What would it take to identify the buyer? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well, now that you mention it, there is something I've been trying to get my hands on. | | | | **Passed**: Identify the buyer |
| Give me the buyer's name or I'll kill you. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: Hasn't Mercer Frey taught you people anything? You kill me and your only contact with the East Empire Company vanishes. That's not smart for business. | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |

If you cannot persuade him, you need to bribe him, although you won't offer him gold as is standard with the bribe option; you have to perform a small theft instead. A buyer of his is looking for [Firebrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebrand_Wine_Case "Skyrim:Firebrand Wine Case"), and there happens to be a case of it up at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"); Gulum-Ei looks to you to steal it for him.

The wine itself is easy enough to retrieve. Once you've walked in through the front door of the Palace, the case of wine is sitting on an end table in a corridor to the left of the main staircase. You will know the case because of the 'Firebrand Wine' label clearly pasted on the side of the crate. Quickly and quietly pocket the wine and head back to the tavern to get your critical information.

### You Didn't Hear It From Me...

When you hand over the wine or were otherwise able to convince him, Gulum-Ei sees fit to compensate you for the effort, and hands over an assortment of [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") as payment. Afterwards, he explains that he was approached by a mysterious woman, who gave him a large sack of gold with which to buy Goldenglow Estate. No name was given, but Gulum-Ei mentions that she was extremely angry, and that this anger was directed at [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") in particular. With nothing else to say on the matter (despite your suspicions to the contrary) Gulum-Ei takes his leave, declaring your business done.

### Tailing the Argonian

You will need to follow Gulum-Ei as he leaves the tavern, as you believe he is not wholly forthcoming about the information he has. If he spots you, he will insist that he told you all he knows, and will tell you to stop following him. Eventually he will lead you to the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), where he works and used to steal goods for the Thieves Guild. Here, you can use the tops of the shelves and stacks to follow him at a close distance without him detecting you, since he will keep to the ground floor. Most of the wall torches lighting the pathways can also be picked up, making it much easier to sneak. The warehouse is also patrolled by [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Warden "Skyrim:East Empire Warden") paid for by the company, and they will attack you on sight. Proceed cautiously and at a distance, as Gulum-Ei is on edge and may occasionally pause to look over his shoulder as if expecting to be followed. Alternatively, you could wait until Gulum-Ei gets far enough ahead of you, and then just kill the wardens if they spot you. Another alternative is to swim in the water, and observe him from there. At the far end of the warehouse, Gulum-Ei will turn around and head back the way he came, so quickly duck out of sight behind a nearby shelf or keg. Gulum-Ei will then take a set of steps down into the water, and around behind a shelving unit to a hidden pathway, leading to a door into [Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto"). If you lose sight of Gulum-Ei, the entrance to Brinewater Grotto can be hard to find. After passing the huge barrel, go down the stairs into the water and really hug the stone wall. You will see a smooth, narrow ramp in the wall that will lead up out of the water by shelving units, then into Brinewater Grotto.

Once you follow him into Brinewater Grotto, the quest will update, instructing you to confront Gulum-Ei; tread carefully, as the cave is littered with traps and bandits. While the Thieves Guild frowns upon killing on the job, the bandits are fair game, and you can either fight them toe-to-toe or systematically take them out with sneak attacks. There is also a chest hidden in the water past the second two guards to the left of the path with some valuable goods in it. When you reach the end of the cave, speak to Gulum-Ei and he will reveal the name of the mysterious antagonist to the Guild: [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah"), the thief who murdered the previous Guildmaster, Gallus.

If you speak to Gulum-Ei again and tell him that he owes you, he will inform you that he will now act as a fence and buy any stolen items you bring to him as his way of repaying you for sparing him.

There are three levers next to the gate. They open the two empty cages and a secret door to the rear of the cavern. Three Horkers may attack in the grotto beyond, but the path leads to the exit to the outside. Return to the Guild for your pay and to tell Mercer your findings. He is (understandably) upset, and deduces where Karliah will be next: a ruin far to the north of Riften known as [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum"). And for this, Mercer insists that he comes along on your [next job](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence")...

### Killing Gulum-Ei

If you do not wish to go to the trouble of tailing the Argonian, you may simply kill him. It is recommended that you kill him stealthily as to avoid incurring a bounty. If and when you kill him you will receive a new objective: "Find alternative source of information." Proceed through the quest exactly as detailed above and where you were supposed to talk to Gulum-Ei there will be a chest with a [written confession](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei%27s_Confession "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei's Confession") instead. If you kill him after following him, the note will be on his body; you must read the note in order to advance to the next objective. If you kill him there is no need to sneak around the guards in either the East Empire Company warehouse or [Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto"). This makes this mission significantly easier to complete for a non-stealthy character, but you will forfeit the payment and you will not have Gulum-Ei as a fence later on.

### Reward

[Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") will speak with [Tonilia](/wiki/Skyrim:Tonilia "Skyrim:Tonilia") and arrange to have a piece of your Thieves Guild armor upgraded. Note you only get to pick **one** piece:

- [Thieves Guild Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Armor "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Armor") - +1 Armor, increases carrying capacity from 20 to 35.
- [Thieves Guild Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Boots "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Boots") - +1 Armor, increases Pickpocket from 15 to 25.
- [Thieves Guild Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Gloves "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Gloves") - +1 Armor, increases Lockpick from 15 to 25.
- [Thieves Guild Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Hood "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Hood") - +2 Armor, increases Barter effect from 10% to 15%

## Notes

- If you are friendly with certain members of the Blue Palace, you can take the case of Firebrand Wine without it being marked as stolen.
- The quest marker for the "Follow Gulum-Ei" objective will update automatically, allowing you to follow him at your leisure.
- Being spotted by Gulum-Ei while tailing him will not result in failure. He will just stop until you retreat out of detection range.
- In the office overlooking the warehouse is the [East Empire Shipping Map](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Shipping_Map "Skyrim:East Empire Shipping Map"), which [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") will pay a leveled amount of gold for.
- Gulum-Ei will not be available to trade with until you return to Mercer and finish the quest.

## Bugs

- If you speak to Maven after acquiring the quest, she will offer to pay for the Goldenglow Estate deed. There is no side objective added to your quest, however, nor any dialogue option to sell the deed to her once you have it. **?**
- If you sold or otherwise permanently misplaced all elements of Thieves Guild Armor, Tonilia will be permanently stuck in the upgrade dialogue, effectively removing her as a fence from the game.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - As of patch 1.4, all pieces of Thieves Guild armor are also available in [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern"). If you have also sold all of those pieces, just wait somewhere outside of the Ragged Flagon, then return and obtain a newly-spawned copy.
- Sometimes after leaving The Winking Skeever, Gulum-Ei will disappear. The quest objective marker shows his location as through the wall of the city, although leaving the city puts the marker on a small door between the trading company and the lighthouse that leads back into Solitude. Another bug of the same kind shows him on a small boat out in the bay.
  -  You can either open the console just after leaving the Winking Skeever and type `prid 000198B7` followed by `moveto player` to move him back inside the walls to your location, proceed to Brinewater Grotto to the room with 3 switches and use the same code (`prid 000198B7` followed by `moveto player`) or try loading a game few times again. Do not try talking to him elsewhere before this point, as it will glitch the quest completion.
- If you speak with Gulum-Ei and get to the point where you should follow him after you have taken Solitude as a Stormcloak, he doesn't ever leave the Winking Skeever.
  - This is solved by waiting for the next day in another location.
- It is possible for Gulum-Ei to disappear after entering the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"). Upon doing so, he will appear in what appears to be a random place, such as on the road north of [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto").
- If you visit the warehouse and kill all the wardens just prior to speaking to [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") and following him, even if you dispose of the bodies in the water, it may cause issues with him walking through the warehouse. He may stop partway and not continue at all, causing a reload before you entered, he may frequently pause and comment that he's going to "find out who did this", or he may walk all the way to the end before returning to the concealed entrance to *Brinewater Grotto*. **?**
- After the quest, Gulum-Ei is supposed to begin fencing goods but is unable to do so because his chest's enable parent setup is wrong.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- Confronting Gulum-Ei doesn't update your quest journal to reflect the new information.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, addresses this issue. The journal entry for stage 200 should also have been in stage 60. That log entry has now been copied to stage 60.

## Quest Stages

| Scoundrel's Folly (TG04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | After the revelations at Honningbrew Meadery and Goldenglow Farm, it's time to put the pieces together and shed some light on the Thieves Guild's anonymous adversary. *Objective 10:* Speak to Mercer Frey |
| 20 |  | Mercer Frey has pointed to Solitude as my next destination. I'm to meet up with an old Argonian contact for the Guild named Gulum-Ei. It's hoped he'll be able to identify the Thieves Guild's anonymous adversary. *Objective 20:* (Optional) Speak to Brynjolf  *Objective 30:* Speak to Gulum-Ei |
| 35 |  | *Objective 35:* Steal case of Firebrand Wine |
| 36 |  | *Objective 37:* Get information from Gulum-Ei |
| 37 |  | *Objective 37:* Get information from Gulum-Ei |
| 40 |  | As predicted by Mercer Frey, Gulum-Ei proved to be quite stubborn and refused to reveal any useful information. I have no choice but to shadow him during his daily routine and discover if he's up to anything that could be used as influence to make him divulge the truth. *Objective 40:* Shadow Gulum-Ei |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Confront Gulum-Ei |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Return to Mercer Frey |
| 200 | ☑ | Thanks to Gulum-Ei's confession, a former member of the Thieves Guild named Karliah has been identified as its anonymous adversary. Worse still, I've discovered that she was the same Dunmer who murdered Gallus, the Guild's previous Guild Master and who's apparently resurfaced after all these years to do the same to Mercer Frey. |
| 55 |  | *Objective 55:* Find alternative source of information |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 30, 42, 45.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG04`.

# Skyrim:Scripted Deaths

## Overview

This article provides a list of all Skyrim [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") who die because of a **scripted death** at some point in the game. A scripted death is one where a game script forcibly kills the character, no matter what choice the player makes. Scripted deaths are usually caused by a quest. [Essential NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") are not immune to scripted deaths, though their essential status must be removed before the death script takes place.

## Guaranteed Deaths

:   *Note that all NPCs die at some point during the listed quest unless stated.*

## Conditional Deaths

These characters will only be killed by a scripted death under certain circumstances. The relevant quest page provides details on whether the character can survive the quest, or whether the character dies in some other way.

:   *Note that all NPCs die at some point during the listed quest unless stated.*

# Skyrim:Scroll Scouting

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Obtain information on the Dragon Elder Scroll.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") or [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | DLC1VQElderHandler |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") or [Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)") | **Concurrent** [Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure") | **Next →** None | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") or [Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)") | | Concurrent | [Seeking Disclosure](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeking_Disclosure "Skyrim:Seeking Disclosure") | | → Next | None | | |

Find the third Elder Scroll required

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") *or* Speak to [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus") at [his outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost")

## Detailed Walkthrough

After the completion of the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet "Skyrim:Prophet"), you will be told by [Dexion Evicus](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") that all three Elder Scrolls must be obtained in order for him to read the whole prophecy and points you towards the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") to gather more information.

Gain access to the College by either passing [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda")'s test or persuading her to let you through (requires a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of 100), and head to the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). Here you will find [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"), who will fill you in on some of the Elder Scrolls lore and bring out two books for you: *[Effects of the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Effects_of_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Effects of the Elder Scrolls")* and *[Ruminations on the Elder Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruminations_on_the_Elder_Scrolls "Skyrim:Ruminations on the Elder Scrolls")*.

Reading the latter starts the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"); once you speak to Urag about [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus"), this quest will be completed. Alternatively, you can skip the College and head directly to [Septimus Signus's Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus%27s_Outpost "Skyrim:Septimus Signus's Outpost") and talk to the man himself, which will also complete this quest.

If you have already obtained and subsequently sold the Elder Scroll to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") (only possible after completing [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")), you must buy back the Elder Scroll. He'll sell it back for 4,000 gold, but he can be persuaded to sell it for half price if you are the Arch-Mage or 3,000 gold if you aren't.

## Notes

- If you're doing Discerning the Transmundane as part of this quest and have Serana with you, you may want to avoid Alftand to get to Blackreach, as she will frequently raise nearby corpses, including the ones you'll want later, during the blood harvest portion of that quest.

## Quest Stages

| Scroll Scouting (DLC1VQElderHandler) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | In order to discover the location of Auriel's Bow, I need to acquire the Elder Scroll that foretells the interactions of the dragons with the history of Nirn. In order to begin my search, I've been told to ask at the College of Winterhold. *Objective 10:* Discover the location of the Elder Scroll (Dragon) |
| 30 |  | In order to discover the location of Auriel's Bow, I need to acquire the Elder Scroll that foretells the interactions of the dragons with the history of Nirn. Having sold that particular scroll to Urag gro-Shub at the College of Winterhold, I'll need to return there to see if he's willing to sell it back. *Objective 20:* Buy back the Elder Scroll (Dragon) from Urag gro-Shub |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully made contact with Urag gro-Shub at the College of Winterhold regarding the Elder Scroll that foretells the interactions of the dragons with the history of Nirn. |
| ☑ | I've successfully purchased the Elder Scroll that foretells the interactions of the dragons with the history of Nirn from Urag gro-Shub at the College of Winterhold. |
| ☑ | I've successfully made contact with a strange old man named Septimus Signus who appears to have information regarding the Elder Scroll that foretells the interactions of the dragons with the history of Nirn. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQElderHandler stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQElderHandler`.

# Skyrim:Sea Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Settlement: Sea Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"), [Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| JaphetsFolly01 | |
| Region | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Location | |
| Beneath [Japhet's Folly Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly_Towers "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly Towers") | |

Sea Cave (Japhet's Folly)

The **Sea Cave** is a cave located in the [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly") area. The cave leads to the lower section of Japhet's Folly Towers.

Entering the Sea Cave

It is featured in the [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") quest. Its entrance is beneath the cliffs, and is reached by crossing the frozen sea (if it is difficult to see, check the local map).

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Sea Cave

The entrance leads directly into the cave, which is used for bringing in provisions via rowboat. It is home to two [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"). There are numerous crates, barrels, and sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") throughout the cave, some of which have bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") or [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top. Against the west wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). A path leading up to a short passage is to the south. This leads into a second room with more crates, barrels, and sacks, and also a hole through a wall opposite into a fort. There is another mudcrab in this second room, and any noise will alert a [Blood Horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker") guard that is standing beyond the hole in the wall, helpfully facing away from you unless alerted to your presence.

Through the hole is a storeroom containing a large stack of unusable barrels, several crates and sacks containing food, and two sets of shelves holding seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Hanging from the ceiling from racks are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, and four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). There is an unlocked chest against the rear wall, and in the southwestern corner is a flight of stairs leading up to a wooden door that leads to [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly").

## Bugs

- [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly") has many severe glitches. See the Japhet's Folly page for more details.
- Beware a glitch that occurs when returning to Japhet's Folly via the Sea Cave after the bombardment has started. The door through which you come will now be disabled, preventing you from going back the way you came, but the top section of the tower is now barred by rubble, leaving you trapped in the bottom section.

# Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Sea of Ghosts ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+of+Ghosts)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts")) | | |
| Regions | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Location | |
| Northern Skyrim | |

The Sea of Ghosts along the northern coast of Skyrim

The **Sea of Ghosts** is a vast ocean to the north of Skyrim.

The Sea of Ghosts is part of the [Padomaic Ocean](/wiki/Lore:Padomaic_Ocean "Lore:Padomaic Ocean"); it meets the [Abecean Sea](/wiki/Lore:Abecean_Sea "Lore:Abecean Sea") off the coast of northwestern [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the [Inner Sea](/wiki/Lore:Inner_Sea "Lore:Inner Sea") along the shores of northern [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"). Some exploration of the sea has yet to be completed, and icebergs are a common sight in its cold, misty waters. The island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim") is located in the Sea of Ghosts, and the island's [Harstrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Harstrad_River "Skyrim:Harstrad River"), [Iggnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Iggnir_River "Skyrim:Iggnir River"), and [Isild](/wiki/Skyrim:Isild_River "Skyrim:Isild River") rivers flow into it. The [Atmorans](/wiki/Lore:Atmoran "Lore:Atmoran") sailed from their homeland, the northern continent of [Atmora](/wiki/Lore:Atmora "Lore:Atmora"), to [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") across this sea.
